{KāSū, 1, 1}
yatra tu naiṣā śaṅkā tā dharmārthakāmebhyo namaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 1.1]
śāstre prakṛtatvāt | [KāSū, 1, 1 2.1]
tatsamayāvabodhakebhyaścācāryebhyaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 3.1]
tatsaṃbandhāt | [KāSū, 1, 1 4.1]
prajāpatir hi prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā tāsāṃ sthitinibandhanaṃ trivargasya sādhanam adhyāyānāṃ śatasahasreṇāgre provāca | [KāSū, 1, 1 5.1]
tasyaikadeśikaṃ manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo dharmādhikārikaṃ pṛthak cakāra | [KāSū, 1, 1 6.1]
bṛhaspatir arthādhikārikam | [KāSū, 1, 1 7.1]
mahādevānucaraśca nandī sahasreṇādhyāyānāṃ pṛthak kāmasūtraṃ provāca | [KāSū, 1, 1 8.1]
tad eva tu pañcabhir adhyāyaśatair auddālakiḥ śvetaketuḥ saṃcikṣepa | [KāSū, 1, 1 9.1]
tad eva tu punar adhyardhenādhyāyaśatena sādhāraṇasāmprayogikakanyāsaṃprayuktakabhāryādhikārikapāradārikavaiśikaupaniṣadikaḥ saptabhir adhikaraṇair bābhravyaḥ pāñcālaḥ saṃcikṣepa | [KāSū, 1, 1 10.1]
tasya ṣaṣṭhaṃ vaiśikam adhikaraṇaṃ pāṭaliputrikāṇāṃ gaṇikānāṃ niyogād dattakaḥ pṛthak cakāra | [KāSū, 1, 1 11.1]
tatprasaṅgāccārāyaṇaḥ sādhāraṇam adhikaraṇaṃ pṛthak provāca | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.1]
suvarṇanābhaḥ sāmprayogikam | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.2]
ghoṭakamukhaḥ kanyāsamprayuktakam | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.3]
gonardīyo bhāryādhikārikam | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.4]
goṇikāputraḥ pāradārikam | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.5]
kucumāra aupaniṣadikam iti | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.6]
evaṃ bahubhir ācāryaistacchāstraṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ praṇītam utsannakalpam abhūt | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.7]
tatra dattakādibhiḥ praṇītānāṃ śāstrāvayavānām ekadeśatvāt mahad iti ca bābhravīyasya duradhyeyatvāt saṃkṣipya sarvam artham alpena granthena kāmasūtram idaṃ praṇītam | [KāSū, 1, 1 12.8]
tasyāyaṃ prakaraṇādhikaraṇasamuddeśaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.1]
śāstrasaṃgrahaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.2]
trivargapratipattiḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.3]
vidyāsamuddeśaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.4]
nāgarikavṛttam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.5]
nāyakasahāyadūtīkarmavimarśaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.6]
iti sādhāraṇaṃ prathamam adhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.7]
adhyāyāḥ pañca | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.8]
prakaraṇāni pañca | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.9]
pramāṇakālabhāvebhyo ratāvasthāpanam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.10]
prītiviśeṣāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.11]
āliṅganavicārāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.12]
cumbanavikalpāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.13]
nakharadanajātayaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.14]
daśanacchedyavidhayaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.15]
deśyā upacārāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.16]
saṃveśanaprakārāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.17]
citraratāni | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.18]
prahaṇanayogāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.19]
tadyuktāśca śītkṛtopakramāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.20]
puruṣāyitam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.21]
puruṣopasṛptāni | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.22]
aupariṣṭakam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.23]
ratārambhāvasānikam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.24]
rataviśeṣāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.25]
praṇayakalahaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.26]
iti sāmprayogikaṃ dvitīyam adhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.27]
adhyāyā daśa | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.28]
prakaraṇāni saptadaśa | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.29]
varaṇavidhānam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.30]
saṃbandhanirṇayaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.31]
kanyāviśrambhaṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.32]
bālāyā upakramāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.33]
iṅgitākārasūcanam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.34]
ekapuruṣābhiyogaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.35]
prayojyasyopāvartanam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.36]
abhiyogataśca kanyāyāḥ pratipattiḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.37]
vivāhayogaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.38]
iti kanyāsamprayuktakaṃ tṛtīyam adhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.39]
adhyāyāḥ pañca | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.40]
prakaraṇāni nava | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.41]
ekacāriṇīvṛttam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.42]
pravāsacaryā | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.43]
sapatnīṣu jyeṣṭhāvṛttam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.44]
kaniṣṭhāvṛttam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.45]
punarbhūvṛttam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.46]
durbhagāvṛttam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.47]
āntaḥpurikam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.48]
puruṣasya bahvīṣu pratipattiḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.49]
iti bhāryādhikārikaṃ caturtham adhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.50]
adhyāyau dvau | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.51]
prakaraṇānyaṣṭau | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.52]
strīpuruṣaśīlāvasthāpanam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.53]
vyāvartanakāraṇāni | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.54]
strīṣu siddhāḥ puruṣāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.55]
ayatnasādhyā yoṣitaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.56]
paricayakāraṇāni | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.57]
abhiyogāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.58]
bhāvaparīkṣā | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.59]
dūtīkarmāṇi | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.60]
īśvarakāmitam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.61]
āntaḥpurikaṃ dārarakṣitakam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.62]
iti pāradārikaṃ pañcamam adhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.63]
adhyāyāḥ ṣaṭ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.64]
prakaraṇāni daśa | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.65]
gamyacintā | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.66]
gamanakāraṇāni | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.67]
upāvartanavidhiḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.68]
kāntānuvartanam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.69]
arthāgamopāyāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.70]
viraktaliṅgāni | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.71]
viraktapratipattiḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.72]
niṣkāsanaprakārāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.73]
viśīrṇapratisaṃdhānam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.74]
lābhaviśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.75]
arthānarthānubandhasaṃśayavicāraḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.76]
veśyāviśeṣāśca | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.77]
iti vaiśikaṃ ṣaṣṭham adhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.78]
adhyāyāḥ ṣaṭ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.79]
prakaraṇāni dvādaśa | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.80]
subhagaṃkaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.81]
vaśīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.82]
vṛṣyāśca yogāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.83]
naṣṭarāgapratyānayanam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.84]
vṛddhividhayaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.85]
citrāśca yogāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.86]
ityaupaniṣadikaṃ saptamam adhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.87]
adhyāyau dvau | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.88]
prakaraṇāni ṣaṭ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.89]
evaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśad adhyāyāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.90]
catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ prakaraṇāni | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.91]
adhikaraṇāni sapta | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.92]
sapādaṃ ślokasahasram | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.93]
iti śāstrasya saṃgrahaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 1 13.94]
saṃkṣepam imam uktvāsya vistaro 'taḥ pravakṣyate | [KāSū, 1, 1 14.1]
iṣṭaṃ hi viduṣāṃ loke samāsavyāsabhāṣaṇam | [KāSū, 1, 1 14.2]
{KāSū, 1, 2}
śatāyur vai puruṣo vibhajya kālam anyonyānubaddhaṃ parasparasyānupaghātakaṃ trivargaṃ seveta | [KāSū, 1, 2 1.1]
bālye vidyāgrahaṇādīn arthān | [KāSū, 1, 2 2.1]
kāmaṃ ca yauvane | [KāSū, 1, 2 3.1]
sthāvire dharmaṃ mokṣaṃ ca | [KāSū, 1, 2 4.1]
anityatvād āyuṣo yathopapādaṃ vā seveta | [KāSū, 1, 2 5.1]
brahmacaryam eva tv ā vidyāgrahaṇāt | [KāSū, 1, 2 6.1]
alaukikatvād adṛṣṭārthatvād apravṛttānāṃ yajñādīnāṃ śāstrāt pravartanam laukikatvād dṛṣṭārthatvācca pravṛttebhyaśca māṃsabhakṣaṇādibhyaḥ śāstrād eva nivāraṇaṃ dharmaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 7.1]
taṃ śruter dharmajñasamavāyāc ca pratipadyeta | [KāSū, 1, 2 8.1]
vidyābhūmihiraṇyapaśudhānyabhāṇḍopaskaramitrādīnām arjanam arjitasya vivardhanam arthaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 9.1]
tam adhyakṣapracārād vārtāsamayavidbhyo vaṇigbhyaśceti | [KāSū, 1, 2 10.1]
śrotratvakcakṣurjihvāghrāṇānām ātmasaṃyuktena manasādhiṣṭhitānāṃ sveṣu sveṣu viṣayeṣv ānukūlyataḥ pravṛttiḥ kāmaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 11.1]
sparśaviśeṣaviṣayāt tv asyābhimānikasukhānuviddhā phalavatyarthapratītiḥ prādhānyāt kāmaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 12.1]
taṃ kāmasūtrān nāgarikajanasamavāyāc ca pratipadyeta | [KāSū, 1, 2 13.1]
eṣāṃ samavāye pūrvaḥ pūrvo garīyān | [KāSū, 1, 2 14.1]
arthaśca rājñaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 15.1]
tanmūlatvāllokayātrāyāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 15.2]
veśyāyāśceti trivargapratipattiḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 15.3]
dharmasyālaukikatvāt tadabhidhāyakaṃ śāstraṃ yuktam | [KāSū, 1, 2 16.1]
upāyapūrvakatvād arthasiddheḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 16.2]
upāyapratipattiḥ śāstrāt | [KāSū, 1, 2 16.3]
tiryagyoniṣvapi tu svayaṃ pravṛttatvāt kāmasya nityatvācca na śāstreṇa kṛtyam astītyācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 17.1]
saṃprayogaparādhīnatvāt strīpuṃsayor upāyam apekṣate | [KāSū, 1, 2 18.1]
sā copāyapratipattiḥ kāmasūtrād iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 19.1]
tiryagyoniṣu punar anāvṛtatvāt strījāteśca ṛtau yāvadarthaṃ pravṛtter abuddhipūrvakatvācca pravṛttīnām anupāyaḥ pratyayaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 20.1]
na dharmāṃścaret | [KāSū, 1, 2 21.1]
eṣyatphalatvāt sāṃśayikatvācca | [KāSū, 1, 2 21.2]
ko hyabāliśo hastagataṃ paragataṃ kuryāt | [KāSū, 1, 2 22.1]
varam adya kapotaḥ śvo mayūrāt | [KāSū, 1, 2 23.1]
varaṃ sāṃśayikān niṣkād asāṃśayikaḥ kārṣāpaṇaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 24.1]
iti laukāyatikāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 24.2]
śāstrasyānabhiśaṅkyatvād abhicārānuvyāhārayośca kvacit phaladarśanān nakṣatracandrasūryatārāgrahacakrasya lokārthaṃ buddhipūrvakam iva pravṛtter darśanād varṇāśramācārasthitilakṣaṇatvāc ca lokayātrāyā hastagatasya ca bījasya bhaviṣyataḥ sasyārthe tyāgadarśanāccared dharmān iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 25.1]
nārthāṃścaret | [KāSū, 1, 2 26.1]
prayatnato 'pi hyete anuṣṭhīyamānā naiva kadācit syuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 26.2]
ananuṣṭhīyamānā api yadṛcchayā bhaveyuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 26.3]
tatsarvaṃ kālakāritam iti | [KāSū, 1, 2 27.1]
kāla eva hi puruṣān arthānarthayor jayaparājayayoḥ sukhaduḥkhayośca sthāpayati | [KāSū, 1, 2 28.1]
kālena balir indraḥ kṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 29.1]
kālena vyavaropitaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 29.2]
kāla eva punar apyenaṃ karteti kālakāraṇikāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 29.3]
puruṣakārapūrvakatvāt sarvapravṛttīnām upāyaḥ pratyayaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 30.1]
avaśyaṃ bhāvino 'pyarthasyopāyapūrvakatvād eva | [KāSū, 1, 2 31.1]
na niṣkarmaṇo bhadram astīti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 31.2]
na kāmāṃścaret | [KāSū, 1, 2 32.1]
dharmārthayoḥ pradhānayor evam anyeṣāṃ ca satāṃ pratyanīkatvāt | [KāSū, 1, 2 32.2]
anarthajanasaṃsargam asadvyavasāyam aśaucam anāyatiṃ caite puruṣasya janayanti | [KāSū, 1, 2 32.3]
tathā pramādaṃ lāghavam apratyayam agrāhyatāṃ ca | [KāSū, 1, 2 33.1]
bahavaśca kāmavaśagāḥ sagaṇā eva vinaṣṭāḥ śrūyante | [KāSū, 1, 2 33.2]
yathā dāṇḍakyo nāma bhojaḥ kāmād brāhmaṇakanyām abhimanyamānaḥ sabandhurāṣṭro vinanāśa | [KāSū, 1, 2 34.1]
devarājaścāhalyām atibalaśca kīcako draupadīṃ rāvaṇaśca sītām apare cānye ca bahavo dṛśyante kāmavaśagā vinaṣṭā ityarthacintakāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 35.1]
śarīrasthitihetutvād āhārasadharmāṇo hi kāmāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 36.1]
phalabhūtāśca dharmārthayoḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 36.2]
boddhavyaṃ tu doṣeṣviva | [KāSū, 1, 2 37.1]
na hi bhikṣukāḥ santīti sthālyo nādhiśrīyante | [KāSū, 1, 2 37.2]
na hi mṛgāḥ santīti yavā nopyanta iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 37.3]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 38.1]
evam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca dharmaṃ copācaran naraḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 38.2]
ihāmutra ca niḥśalyam atyantaṃ sukham aśnute | [KāSū, 1, 2 38.3]
kiṃ syāt paratretyāśaṅkā kārye yasmin na jāyate | [KāSū, 1, 2 39.1]
na cārthaghnaṃ sukhaṃ ceti śiṣṭāstatra vyavasthitāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 39.2]
trivargasādhakaṃ yat syād dvayor ekasya vā punaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 2 40.1]
kāryaṃ tad api kurvīta na tv ekārthaṃ dvibādhakam | [KāSū, 1, 2 40.2]
{KāSū, 1, 3}
dharmārthāṅgavidyākālān anuparodhayan kāmasūtraṃ tadaṅgavidyāśca puruṣo 'dhīyīta | [KāSū, 1, 3 1.1]
prāgyauvanāt strī | [KāSū, 1, 3 2.1]
prattā ca patyur abhiprāyāt | [KāSū, 1, 3 2.2]
yoṣitāṃ śāstragrahaṇasyābhāvād anarthakam iha śāstre strīśāsanam ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 2.3]
prayogagrahaṇaṃ tvāsām | [KāSū, 1, 3 3.1]
prayogasya ca śāstrapūrvakatvād iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 3.2]
tan na kevalam ihaiva | [KāSū, 1, 3 4.1]
sarvatra hi loke katicid eva śāstrajñāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 4.2]
sarvajanaviṣayaśca prayogaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 4.3]
prayogasya ca dūrastham api śāstram eva hetuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 5.1]
asti vyākaraṇam ityavaiyākaraṇā api yājñikā ūhaṃ kratuṣu prayuñjate | [KāSū, 1, 3 6.1]
asti jyautiṣam iti puṇyāheṣu karma kurvate | [KāSū, 1, 3 7.1]
tathāśvārohā gajārohāścāśvān gajāṃścānadhigataśāstrā api vinayante | [KāSū, 1, 3 8.1]
tathāsti rājeti dūrasthā api janapadā na maryādām ativartante tadvad etat | [KāSū, 1, 3 9.1]
santyapi khalu śāstraprahatabuddhayo gaṇikā rājaputryo mahāmātraduhitaraśca | [KāSū, 1, 3 10.1]
tasmād vaiśvāsikājjanād rahasi prayogāñchāstram ekadeśaṃ vā strī gṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 1, 3 11.1]
abhyāsaprayojyāṃśca cātuḥṣaṣṭikān yogān kanyā rahasyekākinyabhyaset | [KāSū, 1, 3 12.1]
ācāryāstu kanyānāṃ pravṛttapuruṣasaṃprayogā sahasampravṛddhā dhātreyikā | [KāSū, 1, 3 13.1]
tathābhūtā vā niratyayasaṃbhāṣaṇā sakhī | [KāSū, 1, 3 13.2]
savayāśca mātṛṣvasā | [KāSū, 1, 3 13.3]
viśrabdhā tatsthānīyā vṛddhadāsī | [KāSū, 1, 3 13.4]
pūrvasaṃsṛṣṭā vā bhikṣukī | [KāSū, 1, 3 13.5]
svasā ca viśvāsaprayogāt | [KāSū, 1, 3 13.6]
gītaṃ vādyaṃ nṛtyaṃ ālekhyaṃ viśeṣakachedyaṃ taṇḍulakusumavalivikārāḥ puṣpāstaraṇaṃ daśanavasanāṅgarāgaḥ maṇibhūmikākarma śayanaracanam udakavādyam udakāghātaḥ citrāśca yogāḥ mālyagrathanavikalpāḥ śekharakāpīḍayojanaṃ nepathyaprayogāḥ karṇapattrabhaṅgāḥ gandhayuktiḥ bhūṣaṇayojanam aindrajālāḥ kaucumārāś ca yogāḥ hastalāghavaṃ vicitraśākayūṣabhakṣyavikārakriyā pānakarasarāgāsavayojanaṃ sūcīvānakarmāṇi sūtrakrīḍā vīṇāḍamarukavādyāni prahelikā pratimālā durvācakayogāḥ pustakavācanaṃ nāṭakākhyāyikādarśanaṃ kāvyasamasyāpūraṇaṃ paṭṭikāvetravānavikalpāḥ takṣakarmāṇi takṣaṇaṃ vāstuvidyā rūpyaratnaparīkṣā dhātuvādaḥ maṇirāgākarajñānaṃ vṛkṣāyurvedayogāḥ meṣakukkuṭalāvakayuddhavidhiḥ śukasārikāpralāpanam utsādane saṃvāhane keśamardane ca kauśalyaṃ akṣaramuṣṭikākathanaṃ mlecchitavikalpāḥ deśabhāṣāvijñānaṃ puṣpaśakaṭikā nimittajñānaṃ yantramātṛkā dhāraṇamātṛkā sampāṭhyaṃ mānasī kāvyakriyā abhidhānakośaḥ chandojñānaṃ kriyākalpaḥ chalitakayogāḥ vastragopanāni dyūtaviśeṣā ākarṣakrīḍā bālakrīḍanakāni vainayikīnāṃ vaijayikīnāṃ vyāyāmikīnāṃ ca vidyānāṃ jñānam iti catuḥṣaṣṭir aṅgavidyāḥ kāmasūtrasyāvayavinyaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 14.1]
pāñcālikī ca catuḥṣaṣṭir aparā | [KāSū, 1, 3 15.1]
tasyāḥ prayogān anvavetya sāṃprayogike vakṣyāmaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 15.2]
kāmasya tadātmakatvāt | [KāSū, 1, 3 15.3]
ābhir abhyucchritā veśyā śīlarūpaguṇānvitā | [KāSū, 1, 3 16.1]
labhate gaṇikāśabdaṃ sthānaṃ ca janasaṃsadi | [KāSū, 1, 3 16.2]
pūjitā sā sadā rājñā guṇavadbhiśca saṃstutā | [KāSū, 1, 3 17.1]
prārthanīyābhigamyā ca lakṣyabhūtā ca jāyate | [KāSū, 1, 3 17.2]
yogajñā rājaputrī ca mahāmātrasutā tathā | [KāSū, 1, 3 18.1]
sahasrāntaḥpunar api svavaśe kurute patim | [KāSū, 1, 3 18.2]
tathā pativiyoge ca vyasanaṃ dāruṇaṃ gatā | [KāSū, 1, 3 19.1]
deśāntare api vidyābhiḥ sā sukhenaiva jīvati | [KāSū, 1, 3 19.2]
naraḥ kalāsu kuśalo vācālaścāṭukārakaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 3 20.1]
asaṃstuto 'pi nārīṇāṃ cittam āśv eva vindati | [KāSū, 1, 3 20.2]
kalānāṃ grahaṇād eva saubhāgyam upajāyate | [KāSū, 1, 3 21.1]
deśakālau tvapekṣyāsāṃ prayogaḥ sambhavenna vā | [KāSū, 1, 3 21.2]
{KāSū, 1, 4}
gṛhītavidyaḥ pratigrahajayakrayanirveśādhigatair arthair anvayāgatair ubhayair vā gārhasthyam adhigamya nāgarakavṛttaṃ varteta | [KāSū, 1, 4 1.1]
nagare pattane kharvaṭe mahati vā sajjanāśraye sthānam | [KāSū, 1, 4 2.1]
yātrāvaśād vā | [KāSū, 1, 4 2.2]
tatra bhavanam āsannodakaṃ vṛkṣavāṭikāvad vibhaktakarmakakṣaṃ dvivāsagṛhaṃ kārayet | [KāSū, 1, 4 3.1]
bāhye ca vāsagṛhe suślakṣṇam ubhayopadhānaṃ madhye vinataṃ śuklottaracchadaṃ śayanīyaṃ syāt | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.1]
pratiśayyikā ca | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.2]
tasya śirobhāge kūrcasthānam vedikā ca | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.3]
tatra rātriśeṣam anulepanaṃ mālyaṃ sikthakaraṇḍakaṃ saugandhikapuṭikā mātuluṅgatvacastāmbūlāni ca syuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.4]
bhūmau patadgrahaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.5]
nāgadantāvasaktā vīṇā | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.6]
citraphalakam | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.7]
vartikāsamudgakaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.8]
yaḥ kaścit pustakaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.9]
kuraṇṭakamālāśca | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.10]
nātidūre bhūmau vṛttāstaraṇaṃ samastakam | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.11]
ākarṣaphalakaṃ dyūtaphalakaṃ ca | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.12]
tasya bahiḥ krīḍāśakunipañjarāṇi | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.13]
ekānte ca takṣatakṣaṇasthānam anyāsāṃ ca krīḍānām | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.14]
svāstīrṇā preṅkhādolā vṛkṣavāṭikāyāṃ sapracchāyā | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.15]
sthaṇḍilapīṭhikā ca sakusumeti bhavanavinyāsaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 4.16]
sa prātar utthāya kṛtaniyatakṛtyaḥ gṛhītadantadhāvanaḥ mātrayānulepanaṃ dhūpaṃ srajam iti ca gṛhītvā dattvā sikthakam alaktakaṃ ca dṛṣṭvādarśe mukham gṛhītamukhavāsatāmbūlaḥ kāryāṇyanutiṣṭhet | [KāSū, 1, 4 5.1]
nityaṃ snānam | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.1]
dvitīyakam utsādanam | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.2]
tṛtīyakaḥ phenakaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.3]
caturthakam āyuṣyam | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.4]
pañcamakaṃ daśamakaṃ vā pratyāyuṣyam ityahīnam | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.5]
sātatyācca saṃvṛtakakṣāsvedāpanodaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.6]
pūrvāhṇāparāhṇayor bhojanam | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.7]
sāyaṃ cārāyaṇasya | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.8]
bhojanānantaraṃ śukasārikāpralāpanavyāpārāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.9]
lāvakakukkuṭameṣayuddhāni | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.10]
tāstāśca kalākrīḍāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.11]
pīṭhamardaviṭavidūṣakāyattā vyāpārāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.12]
divāśayyā ca | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.13]
gṛhītaprasādhanasyāparāhṇe goṣṭhīvihārāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.14]
pradoṣe ca saṃgītakāni | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.15]
tadante ca prasādhite vāsagṛhe saṃcāritasurabhidhūpe sasahāyasya śayyāyām abhisārikāṇāṃ pratīkṣaṇam dūtīnāṃ preṣaṇam svayaṃ vā gamanam | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.16]
āgatānāṃ ca manoharair ālāpair upacāraiśca sasahāyasyopakramāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.17]
varṣapramṛṣṭanepathyānāṃ durdinābhisārikāṇāṃ svayam eva punar maṇḍanam mitrajanena vā paricaraṇam ityāhorātrikam | [KāSū, 1, 4 6.18]
ghaṭānibandhanam goṣṭhīsamavāyaḥ samāpānakam udyānagamanam samasyāḥ krīḍāśca pravartayet | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.1]
pakṣasya māsasya vā prajñāte ahani sarasvatyā bhavane niyuktānāṃ nityaṃ samājaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.2]
kuśīlavāścāgantavaḥ prekṣaṇakam eṣāṃ dadyuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.3]
dvitīye ahani tebhyaḥ pūjā niyataṃ labheran | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.4]
tato yathāśraddham eṣāṃ darśanam utsargo vā | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.5]
vyasanotsaveṣu caiṣāṃ parasparasyaikakāryatā | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.6]
āgantūnāṃ ca kṛtasamavāyānāṃ pūjanam abhyupapattiśca | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.7]
iti gaṇadharmaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.8]
etena taṃ taṃ devatāviśeṣam uddiśya saṃbhāvitasthitayo ghaṭā vyākhyātāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 7.9]
veśyābhavane sabhāyām anyatamasyodavasite vā samānavidyābuddhiśīlavittavayasāṃ saha veśyābhir anurūpair ālāpair āsanabandho goṣṭhī | [KāSū, 1, 4 8.1]
tatra caiṣāṃ kāvyasamasyā kalāsamasyā vā | [KāSū, 1, 4 8.2]
tasyām ujjvalā lokakāntāḥ pūjyāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 8.3]
prītisamānāś cāhāritāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 8.4]
parasparabhavaneṣu cāpānakāni | [KāSū, 1, 4 9.1]
tatra madhumaireyasurāsavān vividhalavaṇaphalaharitaśākatiktakaṭukāmlopadaṃśān veśyāḥ pāyayeyur anupibeyuśca | [KāSū, 1, 4 10.1]
etenodyānagamanaṃ vyākhyātam | [KāSū, 1, 4 10.2]
pūrvāhṇa eva svalaṃkṛtāsturagādhirūḍhā veśyābhiḥ saha paricārakānugatā gaccheyuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 11.1]
daivasikīṃ ca yātrāṃ tatrānubhūya kukkuṭayuddhadyūtaiḥ prekṣābhir anukūlaiśca ceṣṭitaiḥ kālaṃ gamayitvā aparāhṇe gṛhītatadudyānopabhogacihnāstathaiva pratyāvrajeyuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 11.2]
etena racitodgrāhodakānāṃ grīṣme jalakrīḍāgamanaṃ vyākhyātam | [KāSū, 1, 4 11.3]
yakṣarātriḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 12.1]
kaumudījāgaraḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 12.2]
suvasantakaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 12.3]
sahakārabhañjikā abhyūṣakhādikā bisakhādikā navapattrikā udakakṣveḍikā pāñcālānuyānam ekaśālmalī kadambayuddhāni tāstāśca māhimānyo deśyāśca krīḍā janebhyo viśiṣṭam ācareyuḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 13.1]
iti sambhūya krīḍāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 13.2]
ekacāriṇaśca vibhavasāmarthyād gaṇikāyā nāyikāyāśca sakhībhir nāgarakaiśca saha caritam etena vyākhyātam | [KāSū, 1, 4 14.1]
avibhavastu śarīramātro mallikāphenakakaṣāyamātraparicchadaḥ pūjyād deśād āgataḥ kalāsu vicakṣaṇastadupadeśena goṣṭhyāṃ veśocite ca vṛtte sādhayed ātmānam iti pīṭhamardaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 15.1]
bhuktavibhavastu guṇavān sakalatro veśe goṣṭhyāṃ ca bahumatas tadupajīvī ca viṭaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 16.1]
ekadeśavidyastu krīḍanako viśvāsyaśca vidūṣakaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 17.1]
vaihāsiko vā | [KāSū, 1, 4 17.2]
ete veśyānāṃ nāgarakāṇāṃ ca mantriṇaḥ saṃdhivigrahaniyuktāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 17.3]
tair bhikṣukyaḥ kalāvidagdhā muṇḍā vṛṣalyo vṛddhagaṇikāśca vyākhyātāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 18.1]
grāmavāsī ca sajātān vicakṣaṇān kautūhalikān protsāhya nāgarakajanasya vṛttaṃ varṇayañ śraddhāṃ ca janayaṃstad evānukurvīta | [KāSū, 1, 4 19.1]
goṣṭhīśca pravartayet | [KāSū, 1, 4 19.2]
saṃgatyā janam anurañjayet | [KāSū, 1, 4 19.3]
karmasu ca sāhāyyena cānugṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 1, 4 19.4]
upakārayecca | [KāSū, 1, 4 19.5]
iti nāgarakavṛttam | [KāSū, 1, 4 19.6]
nātyantaṃ saṃskṛtenaiva nātyantaṃ deśabhāṣayā | [KāSū, 1, 4 20.1]
kathāṃ goṣṭhīṣu kathayaṃlloke bahumato bhavet | [KāSū, 1, 4 20.2]
yā goṣṭhī lokavidviṣṭā yā ca svairavisarpiṇī | [KāSū, 1, 4 21.1]
parahiṃsātmikā yā ca na tām avatared budhaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 4 21.2]
lokacittānuvartinyā krīḍāmātraikakāryayā | [KāSū, 1, 4 22.1]
goṣṭhyā sahacaran vidvāṃlloke siddhiṃ niyacchati | [KāSū, 1, 4 22.2]
{KāSū, 1, 5}
kāmaścaturṣu varṇeṣu savarṇataḥ śāstrataścānanyapūrvāyāṃ prayujyamānaḥ putrīyo yaśasyo laukikaśca bhavati | [KāSū, 1, 5 1.1]
tadviparīta uttamavarṇāsu paraparigṛhītāsu ca | [KāSū, 1, 5 2.1]
pratiṣiddho 'varavarṇāsvaniravasitāsu | [KāSū, 1, 5 2.2]
veśyāsu punarbhūṣu ca na śiṣṭo na pratiṣiddhaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 2.3]
sukhārthatvāt | [KāSū, 1, 5 2.4]
tatra nāyikāstisraḥ kanyā punarbhūr veśyā ca | [KāSū, 1, 5 3.1]
iti | [KāSū, 1, 5 3.2]
anyakāraṇavaśāt paraparigṛhītāpi pākṣikī caturthīti goṇikāputraḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 4.1]
sa yadā manyate svairiṇīyam | [KāSū, 1, 5 5.1]
anyato 'pi bahuśo vyavasitacāritrā tasyāṃ veśyāyām iva gamanam uttamavarṇinyām api na dharmapīḍāṃ kariṣyati | [KāSū, 1, 5 6.1]
punarbhūr iyam | [KāSū, 1, 5 6.2]
anyapūrvāvaruddhā nātra śaṅkāsti | [KāSū, 1, 5 7.1]
patiṃ vā mahāntam īśvaram asmadamitrasaṃsṛṣṭam iyam avagṛhya prabhutvena carati | [KāSū, 1, 5 8.1]
sā mayā saṃsṛṣṭā snehād enaṃ vyāvartayiṣyati | [KāSū, 1, 5 8.2]
virasaṃ vā mayi śaktam apakartukāmaṃ ca prakṛtim āpādayiṣyati | [KāSū, 1, 5 9.1]
tayā vā mitrīkṛtena mitrakāryam amitrapratīghātam anyad vā duṣpratipādakaṃ kāryaṃ sādhayiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 1, 5 10.1]
saṃsṛṣṭo vānayā hatvāsyāḥ patim asmadbhāvyaṃ tadaiśvaryam evam adhigamiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 1, 5 11.1]
niratyayaṃ vāsyā gamanam arthānubaddham | [KāSū, 1, 5 12.1]
ahaṃ ca niḥsāratvāt kṣīṇavṛttyupāyaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 12.2]
so 'ham anenopāyena taddhanam atimahad akṛcchrād adhigamiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 1, 5 12.3]
marmajñā vā mayi dṛḍham abhikāmā sā mām anicchantaṃ doṣavikhyāpanena dūṣayiṣyati | [KāSū, 1, 5 12.4]
asadbhūtaṃ vā doṣaṃ śraddheyaṃ duṣparihāraṃ mayi kṣepsyati yena me vināśaḥ syāt | [KāSū, 1, 5 13.1]
āyatimantaṃ vā vaśyaṃ patiṃ matto vibhidya dviṣataḥ saṃgrāhayiṣyati | [KāSū, 1, 5 14.1]
svayaṃ vā taiḥ saha saṃsṛjyeta | [KāSū, 1, 5 15.1]
madavarodhānāṃ vā dūṣayitā patir asyāstad asyāham api dārān eva dūṣayan pratikariṣyāmi | [KāSū, 1, 5 15.2]
rājaniyogāccāntarvartinaṃ śatruṃ vāsya nirhaniṣyāmi | [KāSū, 1, 5 16.1]
yāmanyāṃ kāmayiṣye sāsyā vaśagā | [KāSū, 1, 5 17.1]
tām anena saṃkrameṇādhigamiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 1, 5 17.2]
kanyām alabhyāṃ vātmādhīnām artharūpavatīṃ mayi saṃkrāmayiṣyati | [KāSū, 1, 5 17.3]
mamāmitro vāsyāḥ patyā sahaikībhāvam upagatastam anayā rasena yojayiṣyāmītyevamādibhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ parastriyam api prakurvīta | [KāSū, 1, 5 17.4]
iti sāhasikyaṃ na kevalaṃ rāgād eva | [KāSū, 1, 5 18.1]
etair eva kāraṇair mahāmātrasambaddhā rājasambaddhā vā tatraikadeśacāriṇī kācid anyā vā kāryasaṃpādinī vidhavā pañcamīti cārāyaṇaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 18.2]
saiva pravrajitā ṣaṣṭhīti suvarṇanābhaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 18.3]
gaṇikāyā duhitā paricārikā vānanyapūrvā saptamīti ghoṭakamukhaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 18.4]
utkrāntabālabhāvā kulayuvatir upacārānyatvād aṣṭamīti gonardīyaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 18.5]
kāryāntarābhāvād etāsām api pūrvāsvevopalakṣaṇam tasmāccatasra eva nāyikā iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 18.6]
bhinnatvāt tṛtīyā prakṛtiḥ pañcamītyeke | [KāSū, 1, 5 18.7]
eka eva tu sārvalaukiko nāyakaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 19.1]
pracchannastu dvitīyaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 19.2]
viśeṣālābhāt | [KāSū, 1, 5 19.3]
uttamādhamamadhyamatāṃ tu guṇāguṇato vidyāt | [KāSū, 1, 5 19.4]
tāṃstūbhayor api guṇāguṇān vaiśike vakṣyāmaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 19.5]
agamyāstvevaitāḥ kuṣṭhinyunmattā patitā bhinnarahasyā prakāśaprārthinī gataprāyayauvanātiśvetātikṛṣṇā durgandhā saṃbandhinī sakhī pravrajitā saṃbandhisakhiśrotriyarājadārāśca | [KāSū, 1, 5 20.1]
dṛṣṭapañcapuruṣā nāgamyā kācid astīti bābhravīyāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 21.1]
saṃbandhisakhiśrotriyarājadāravarjam iti goṇikāputraḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 22.1]
saha pāṃsukrīḍitam upakārasambaddhaṃ samānaśīlavyasanaṃ sahādhyāyinaṃ yaścāsya marmāṇi rahasyāni ca vidyāt yasya cāyaṃ vidyād vā dhātrapatyaṃ sahasaṃvṛddhaṃ mitram | [KāSū, 1, 5 23.1]
pitṛpaitāmaham avisaṃvādakam adṛṣṭavaikṛtaṃ vaśyaṃ dhruvam alobhaśīlam aparihāryam amantravisrāvīti mitrasaṃpat | [KāSū, 1, 5 24.1]
rajakanāpitamālākāragāndhikasaurikabhikṣukagopālakatāmbūlikasauvarṇikapīṭhamardaviṭavidūṣakādayo mitrāṇi | [KāSū, 1, 5 25.1]
tadyoṣinmitrāśca nāgarakāḥ syur iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 25.2]
yad ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇam ubhayatrodāraṃ viśeṣato nāyikāyāḥ suvisrabdhaṃ tatra dūtakarma | [KāSū, 1, 5 26.1]
paṭutā dhārṣṭyam iṅgitākārajñatā pratāraṇakālajñatā viṣahyabuddhitvaṃ laghvī pratipattiḥ sopāyā ceti dūtaguṇāḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 27.1]
bhavati cātra ślokaḥ | [KāSū, 1, 5 28.1]
ātmavān mitravān yukto bhāvajño deśakālavit | [KāSū, 1, 5 28.2]

oṣṭhasaṃdaṃśenāvagṛhyauṣṭhadvayam api cumbeta | [KāSū, 2, 3 18.1]
iti saṃpuṭakaṃ striyāḥ puṃso vā ajātavyañjanasya | [KāSū, 2, 3 18.2]

etena balād vadanaradanagrahaṇaṃ dānaṃ ca vyākhyātam | [KāSū, 2, 3 20.1]
samaṃ pīḍitam añcitaṃ mṛdu śeṣāṅgeṣu cumbanaṃ sthānaviśeṣayogāt | [KāSū, 2, 3 21.1]
iti cumbanaviśeṣāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 3 21.2]
suptasya mukham avalokayantyāḥ svābhiprāyeṇa cumbanaṃ rāgadīpanam | [KāSū, 2, 3 22.1]
pramattasya vivadamānasya vā anyato 'bhimukhasya suptābhimukhasya vā nidrāvyāghātārthaṃ calitakam | [KāSū, 2, 3 23.1]
cirarātrāv āgatasya śayanasuptāyāḥ svābhiprāyacumbanaṃ prātibodhikam | [KāSū, 2, 3 24.1]
sāpi tu bhāvajijñāsārthinī nāyakasyāgamanakālaṃ saṃlakṣya vyājena suptā syāt | [KāSū, 2, 3 25.1]
ādarśe kuḍye salile vā prayojyāyāśchāyācumbanam ākārapradarśanārtham eva kāryam | [KāSū, 2, 3 26.1]
bālasya citrakarmaṇaḥ pratimāyāśca cumbanaṃ saṃkrāntakam āliṅganaṃ ca | [KāSū, 2, 3 27.1]
tathā niśi prekṣaṇake svajanasamāje vā samīpe gatasya prayojyāyā hastāṅgulicumbanaṃ saṃviṣṭasya vā pādāṅgulicumbanam | [KāSū, 2, 3 28.1]
saṃvāhikāyāstu nāyakam ākārayantyā nidrāvaśād akāmāyā iva tasyorvor vadanasya nidhānam ūrucumbanaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhacumbanaṃ cetyābhiyogikāni | [KāSū, 2, 3 29.1]
bhavati cātra ślokaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 3 30.1]

karaṇena ca tenaiva cumbite praticumbitam | [KāSū, 2, 3 30.3]
{KāSū, 2, 4}
rāgavṛddhau saṃgharṣātmakaṃ nakhavilekhanam | [KāSū, 2, 4 1.1]

tadācchuritakam ardhacandro maṇḍalaṃ rekhā vyāghranakhaṃ mayūrapadakaṃ śaśaplutakam utpalapatrakam iti rūpato 'ṣṭavikalpam | [KāSū, 2, 4 4.1]

prayojyāyāṃ ca tasyāṅgasaṃvāhane śirasaḥ kaṇḍūyane piṭakabhedane vyākulīkaraṇe bhīṣaṇena prayogaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 4 13.1]

nābhimūlakakundaravaṅkṣaṇeṣu tasya prayogaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 4 16.1]
sarvasthāneṣu nātidīrghā lekhā | [KāSū, 2, 4 17.1]
saiva vakrā vyāghranakhakam ā stanamukham | [KāSū, 2, 4 18.1]
pañcabhir abhimukhair lekhā cūcukābhimukhī mayūrapadakam | [KāSū, 2, 4 19.1]
tatsaṃprayogaślāghāyāḥ stanacūcuke saṃnikṛṣṭāni pañcanakhapadāni śaśaplutakam | [KāSū, 2, 4 20.1]
stanapṛṣṭhe mekhalāpathe cotpalapattrākṛtītyutpalapatrakam | [KāSū, 2, 4 21.1]

iti nakhakarmāṇi | [KāSū, 2, 4 22.2]
ākṛtivikārayuktāni cānyānyapi kurvīta | [KāSū, 2, 4 23.1]
vikalpānām anantatvād ānantyācca kauśalavidher abhyāsasya ca sarvagāmitvād rāgātmakatvācchedyasya prakārān ko 'bhisamīkṣitum arhatītyācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 4 24.1]
bhavati hi rāge api citrāpekṣā | [KāSū, 2, 4 25.1]
vaicitryācca parasparaṃ rāgo janayitavyaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 4 25.2]

na tu paraparigṛhītāsv evaṃ kuryāt | [KāSū, 2, 4 26.1]
pracchanneṣu pradeśeṣu tāsām anusmaraṇārthaṃ rāgavardhanācca viśeṣān darśayet | [KāSū, 2, 4 26.2]

{KāSū, 2, 5}

{KāSū, 2, 6}
rāgakāle viśālayantyeva jaghanaṃ mṛgī saṃviśed uccarate | [KāSū, 2, 6 1.1]

nyāyyo yatra yogastatra samapṛṣṭham | [KāSū, 2, 6 3.1]

tathā karmayogāt | [KāSū, 2, 6 17.2]

sauvarṇanābhāstu | [KāSū, 2, 6 22.1]

tatkuñcitāv utpīḍitakam | [KāSū, 2, 6 24.1]
tad ekasmin prasārite ardhapīḍitakam | [KāSū, 2, 6 25.1]

ūrdhvāv ūrū vyatyasyed iti pīḍitakam | [KāSū, 2, 6 29.1]
jaṅghāvyatyāsena padmāsanavat | [KāSū, 2, 6 30.1]

tathā sukaratvād iti suvarṇanābhaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 6 32.2]

atha citraratāni | [KāSū, 2, 6 34.1]

teṣām ekaikaśo yugapacca yathāsātmyaṃ yathāyogaṃ ca rañjayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 2, 6 42.2]
eko dhārayed enām anyo niṣeveta | [KāSū, 2, 6 43.1]

{KāSū, 2, 8}

{KāSū, 2, 9}

vyāsastasya ca vijñeyo mukhacumbanavad vidhiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 9 30.2]
parivartitadehau tu strīpuṃsau yat parasparam | [KāSū, 2, 9 31.1]
yugapat samprayujyete sa kāmaḥ kākilaḥ smṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 9 31.2]
tasmād guṇavatastyaktvā caturāṃstyāgino narān | [KāSū, 2, 9 32.1]
veśyāḥ khaleṣu rajyante dāsahastipakādiṣu | [KāSū, 2, 9 32.2]
na tv etad brāhmaṇo vidvān mantrī vā rājadhūrdharaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 9 33.1]
gṛhītapratyayo vāpi kārayed aupariṣṭakam | [KāSū, 2, 9 34.1]
na śāstram astītyetāvat prayoge kāraṇaṃ bhavet | [KāSū, 2, 9 35.1]
śāstrārthān vyāpino vidyāt prayogāṃstv ekadeśikān | [KāSū, 2, 9 35.2]
rasavīryavipākā hi śvamāṃsasyāpi vaidyake | [KāSū, 2, 9 36.1]
kīrtitā iti tat kiṃ syād bhakṣaṇīyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 9 36.2]
santyeva puruṣāḥ kecit santi deśāstathāvidhāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 9 37.1]
santi kālāśca yeṣv ete yogā na syur nirarthakāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 9 37.2]
tasmād deśaṃ ca kālaṃ ca prayogaṃ śāstram eva ca | [KāSū, 2, 9 38.1]
ātmānaṃ cāpi samprekṣya yogān yuñjīta vā na vā | [KāSū, 2, 9 38.2]
arthasyāsya rahasyatvāccalatvān manasastathā | [KāSū, 2, 9 39.1]
kaḥ kadā kiṃ kutaḥ kuryād iti ko jñātum arhati | [KāSū, 2, 9 39.2]
{KāSū, 2, 10}
nāgarakaḥ saha mitrajanena paricārakaiśca kṛtapuṣpopahāre saṃcāritasurabhidhūpe ratyāvāse prasādhite vāsagṛhe kṛtasnānaprasādhanāṃ yuktyā pītāṃ striyaṃ sāntvanaiḥ punaḥ pānena copakramet | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.1]
dakṣiṇataścāsyā upaveśanam | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.2]
keśahaste vastrānte nīvyām ityavalambanam | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.3]
ratyarthaṃ savyena bāhunānuddhataḥ pariṣvaṅgaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.4]
pūrvaprakaraṇasambaddhaiḥ parihāsānurāgair vacobhir anuvṛttiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.5]
gūḍhāślīlānāṃ ca vastūnāṃ samasyayā paribhāṣaṇam | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.6]
sanṛttam anṛttaṃ vā gītaṃ vāditram | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.7]
kalāsu saṃkathāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.8]
punaḥ pānenopacchandanam | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.9]
jātānurāgāyāṃ kusumānulepanatāmbūladānena ca śeṣajanavisṛṣṭiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.10]
vijane ca yathoktair āliṅganādibhir enām uddharṣayet | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.11]
tato nīvīviśleṣaṇādi yathoktam upakrameta | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.12]
ityayaṃ ratārambhaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 1.13]
ratāvasānikaṃ rāgam ativāhyāsaṃstutayor iva savrīḍayoḥ parasparam apaśyatoḥ pṛthak pṛthag ācārabhūmigamanam | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.1]
pratinivṛttya cāvrīḍāyamānayor ucitadeśopaviṣṭayostāmbūlagrahaṇam acchīkṛtaṃ candanam anyad vānulepanaṃ tasyā gātre svayam eva niveśayet | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.2]
savyena bāhunā caināṃ parirabhya caṣakahastaḥ sāntvayan pāyayet | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.3]
jalānupānaṃ vā khaṇḍakhādyakam anyad vā prakṛtisātmyayuktam ubhāvapyupayuñjīyātām | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.4]
accharasakayūṣam amlayavāgūṃ bhṛṣṭamāṃsopadaṃśāni pānakāni cūtaphalāni śuṣkamāṃsaṃ mātuluṅgacukrakāṇi saśarkarāṇi ca yathādeśasātmyaṃ ca | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.5]
tatra madhuram idaṃ mṛdu viśadam iti ca vidaśya vidaśya tat tad upāharet | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.6]
harmyatalasthitayor vā candrikāsevanārtham āsanam | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.7]
tadaṅkasaṃlīnāyāścandramasaṃ paśyantyā nakṣatrapaṅktivyaktīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.8]
arundhatīdhruvasaptarṣimālādarśanaṃ ca | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.9]
iti ratāvasānikam | [KāSū, 2, 10 2.10]
avasāne api ca prītir upacārair upaskṛtā | [KāSū, 2, 10 3.1]
savisrambhakathāyogai ratiṃ janayate parām | [KāSū, 2, 10 3.2]
parasparaprītikarair ātmabhāvānuvartanaiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 4.1]
kṣaṇāt krodhaparāvṛttaiḥ kṣaṇāt prītivilokitaiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 4.2]
hallīsakakrīḍanakair gāyanair lāṭarāsakaiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 5.1]
rāgalolārdranayanaiś candramaṇḍalavīkṣaṇaiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 5.2]
ādye saṃdarśane jāte pūrvaṃ ye syur manorathāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 6.1]
punarviyoge duḥkhaṃ ca tasya sarvasya kīrtanaiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 6.2]
kīrtanānte ca rāgeṇa pariṣvaṅgaiḥ sacumbanaiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 7.1]
taistaiśca bhāvaiḥ saṃyukto yūno rāgo vivardhate | [KāSū, 2, 10 7.2]
rāgavad āhāryarāgaṃ kṛtrimarāgaṃ vyavahitarāgaṃ poṭārataṃ khalaratam ayantritaratam iti rataviśeṣāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 8.1]
saṃdarśanāt prabhṛtyubhayor api pravṛddharāgayoḥ prayatnakṛte samāgame pravāsapratyāgamane vā kalahaviyogayoge tadrāgavat | [KāSū, 2, 10 9.1]
tatrātmābhiprāyād yāvadarthaṃ ca pravṛttiḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 10.1]
madhyastharāgayor ārabdhaṃ yad anurajyate tad āhāryarāgam | [KāSū, 2, 10 11.1]
tatra cātuḥṣaṣṭikair yogaiḥ sātmyānuviddhaiḥ saṃdhukṣya saṃdhukṣya rāgaṃ pravarteta | [KāSū, 2, 10 12.1]
tatkāryahetor anyatra saktayor vā kṛtrimarāgam | [KāSū, 2, 10 12.2]
tatra samuccayena yogāñ śāstrataḥ paśyet | [KāSū, 2, 10 13.1]
puruṣastu hṛdayapriyām anyāṃ manasi nidhāya vyavaharet | [KāSū, 2, 10 14.1]
saṃprayogāt prabhṛti ratiṃ yāvat | [KāSū, 2, 10 14.2]
atastadvyavahitarāgam | [KāSū, 2, 10 14.3]
nyūnāyāṃ kumbhadāsyāṃ paricārikāyāṃ vā yāvadarthaṃ saṃprayogastatpoṭāratam | [KāSū, 2, 10 15.1]
tatropacārān nādriyeta | [KāSū, 2, 10 16.1]
tathā veśyāyā grāmīṇena saha yāvadarthaṃ khalaratam | [KāSū, 2, 10 17.1]
grāmavrajapratyantayoṣidbhiś ca nāgarakasya | [KāSū, 2, 10 18.1]
utpannavisrambhayośca parasparānukūlyād ayantritaratam | [KāSū, 2, 10 19.1]
iti ratāni | [KāSū, 2, 10 19.2]
vardhamānapraṇayā tu nāyikā sapatnīnām agrahaṇaṃ tadāśrayam ālāpaṃ vā gotraskhalitaṃ vā na marṣayet | [KāSū, 2, 10 20.1]
nāyakavyalīkaṃ ca | [KāSū, 2, 10 20.2]
tatra subhṛśaḥ kalaho ruditam āyāsaḥ śiroruhāṇām avakṣodanaṃ prahaṇanam āsanācchayanād vā mahyāṃ patanaṃ mālyabhūṣaṇāvamokṣo bhūmau śayyā ca | [KāSū, 2, 10 21.1]
tatra yuktarūpeṇa sāmnā pādapatanena vā prasannamanāstām anunayann upakramya śayanam ārohayet | [KāSū, 2, 10 22.1]
tasya ca vacanam uttareṇa yojayantī vivṛddhakrodhā sakacagraham asyāsyam unnamayya pādena bāhau śirasi vakṣasi pṛṣṭhe vā sakṛd dvistrir avahanyāt | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.1]
dvāradeśaṃ gacchet | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.2]
tatropaviśyāśrukaraṇam iti | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.3]
atikruddhāpi tu na dvāradeśād bhūyo gacchet | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.4]
doṣavattvāt | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.5]
iti dattakaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.6]
tatra yuktito 'nunīyamānā prasādam ākāṅkṣet | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.7]
prasannāpi tu sakaṣāyair eva vākyair enaṃ tudatīva prasannaratikāṅkṣiṇī nāyakena parirabhyeta | [KāSū, 2, 10 23.8]
svabhavanasthā tu nimittāt kalahitā tathāvidhaceṣṭaiva nāyakam abhigacchet | [KāSū, 2, 10 24.1]
tatra pīṭhamardaviṭavidūṣakair nāyakaprayuktair upaśamitaroṣā tair evānunītā taiḥ sahaiva tadbhavanam adhigacchet | [KāSū, 2, 10 24.2]
tatra ca vaset | [KāSū, 2, 10 24.3]
iti praṇayakalahaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 24.4]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 25.1]
evam etāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ bābhravyeṇa prakīrtitām | [KāSū, 2, 10 25.2]
prayuñjāno varastrīṣu siddhiṃ gacchati nāyakaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 25.3]
bruvann apyanyaśāstrāṇi catuḥṣaṣṭivivarjitaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 26.1]
vidvatsaṃsadi nātyarthaṃ kathāsu paripūjyate | [KāSū, 2, 10 26.2]
varjito 'pyanyavijñānair etayā yastvalaṃkṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 27.1]
sa goṣṭhyāṃ naranārīṇāṃ kathāsvagraṃ vigāhate | [KāSū, 2, 10 27.2]
vidvadbhiḥ pūjitām enāṃ khalair api supūjitām | [KāSū, 2, 10 28.1]
pūjitāṃ gaṇikāsaṃghair nandinīṃ ko na pūjayet | [KāSū, 2, 10 28.2]
nandinī subhagā siddhā subhagaṃkaraṇīti ca | [KāSū, 2, 10 29.1]
nārīpriyeti cācāryaiḥ śāstreṣv eṣā nirucyate | [KāSū, 2, 10 29.2]
kanyābhiḥ parayoṣidbhir gaṇikābhiśca bhāvataḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 30.1]
vīkṣyate bahumānena catuḥṣaṣṭivicakṣaṇaḥ | [KāSū, 2, 10 30.2]
{KāSū, 3, 1}
savarṇāyām ananyapūrvāyāṃ śāstrato 'dhigatāyāṃ dharmo 'rthaḥ putrāḥ saṃbandhaḥ pakṣavṛddhir anupaskṛtā ratiśca | [KāSū, 3, 1 1.1]
tasmāt kanyām abhijanopetāṃ mātāpitṛmatīṃ trivarṣāt prabhṛti nyūnavayasaṃ ślāghyācāre dhanavati pakṣavati kule saṃbandhipriye saṃbandhibhir ākule prasūtāṃ prabhūtamātṛpitṛpakṣāṃ rūpaśīlalakṣaṇasampannām anyūnādhikāvinaṣṭadantanakhakarṇakeśākṣistanīm arogiprakṛtiśarīrāṃ tathāvidha eva śrutavāñ śīlayet | [KāSū, 3, 1 2.1]
yāṃ gṛhītvā kṛtinam ātmānaṃ manyeta na ca samānair nindyeta tasyāṃ pravṛttir iti ghoṭakamukhaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 3.1]
tasyā varaṇe mātāpitarau saṃbandhinaśca prayateran | [KāSū, 3, 1 4.1]
mitrāṇi ca gṛhītavākyānyubhayasambaddhāni | [KāSū, 3, 1 4.2]
tānyanyeṣāṃ varayitṝṇāṃ doṣān pratyakṣānāgamikāṃśca śrāvayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 5.1]
kaulān pauruṣeyān abhiprāyasaṃvardhakāṃśca nāyakaguṇān | [KāSū, 3, 1 5.2]
viśeṣataśca kanyāmātur anukūlāṃstadātvāyatiyuktān darśayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 5.3]
daivacintakarūpaśca śakunanimittagrahalagnabalalakṣaṇadarśanena nāyakasya bhaviṣyantam arthasaṃyogaṃ kalyāṇam anuvarṇayet | [KāSū, 3, 1 6.1]
apare punar asyānyato viśiṣṭena kanyālābhena kanyāmātaram unmādayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 7.1]
daivanimittaśakunopaśrutīnām ānulomyena kanyāṃ varayed dadyācca | [KāSū, 3, 1 8.1]
na yadṛcchayā kevalamānuṣāyeti ghoṭakamukhaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 9.1]
suptāṃ rudatīṃ niṣkrāntāṃ varaṇe parivarjayet | [KāSū, 3, 1 10.1]
apraśastanāmadheyāṃ ca guptāṃ dattāṃ ghonāṃ pṛṣatām ṛṣabhāṃ vinatāṃ vikaṭāṃ vimuṇḍāṃ śucidūṣitāṃ sāṃkarikīṃ rākāṃ phalīnīṃ mitrāṃ svanujām varṣakarīṃ ca varjayet | [KāSū, 3, 1 10.2]
nakṣatrākhyāṃ nadīnāmnīṃ vṛkṣanāmnīṃ ca garhitām | [KāSū, 3, 1 11.1]
lakārarephopāntāṃ ca varaṇe parivarjayet | [KāSū, 3, 1 11.2]
yasyāṃ manaścakṣuṣor nibandhastasyām ṛddhiḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 12.1]
netarām ādriyeta | [KāSū, 3, 1 12.2]
ityeke | [KāSū, 3, 1 12.3]
tasmāt pradānasamaye kanyām udāraveṣāṃ sthāpayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 13.1]
aparāhṇikaṃ ca nityaṃ prasādhitāyāḥ sakhībhiḥ saha krīḍā | [KāSū, 3, 1 13.2]
yajñavivāhādiṣu janasaṃdrāveṣu prāyatnikaṃ darśanam | [KāSū, 3, 1 13.3]
tathotsaveṣu ca | [KāSū, 3, 1 13.4]
paṇyasadharmatvāt | [KāSū, 3, 1 13.5]
varaṇārtham upagatāṃśca bhadradarśanān pradakṣiṇavācaśca tatsaṃbandhisaṃgatān puruṣān maṅgalaiḥ pratigṛhṇīyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 14.1]
kanyāṃ caiṣām alaṃkṛtām anyāpadeśena darśayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 14.2]
daivaṃ parīkṣaṇaṃ cāvadhiṃ sthāpayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 14.3]
ā pradānaniścayāt | [KāSū, 3, 1 14.4]
snānādiṣu niyujyamānā varayitāraḥ sarvaṃ bhaviṣyatītyuktvā na tadaharevābhyupagaccheyuḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 15.1]
deśapravṛttisātmyād vā brāhmaprājāpatyārṣadaivānām anyatamena vivāhena śāstrataḥ pariṇayet | [KāSū, 3, 1 16.1]
iti varaṇavidhānam | [KāSū, 3, 1 16.2]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 17.1]
samasyādyāḥ sahakrīḍā vivāhāḥ saṃgatāni ca | [KāSū, 3, 1 17.2]
samānair eva kāryāṇi nottamair nāpi vādhamaiḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 17.3]
kanyāṃ gṛhītvā varteta preṣyavad yatra nāyakaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 18.1]
taṃ vidyād uccasaṃbandhaṃ parityaktaṃ manasvibhiḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 18.2]
svāmivad vicared yatra bāndhavaiḥ svaiḥ puraskṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 1 19.1]
aślāghyo hīnasaṃbandhaḥ so 'pi sadbhir vinindyate | [KāSū, 3, 1 19.2]
parasparasukhāsvādā krīḍā yatra prayujyate | [KāSū, 3, 1 20.1]
viśeṣayantī cānyonyaṃ saṃbandhaḥ sa vidhīyate | [KāSū, 3, 1 20.2]
kṛtvāpi coccasaṃbandhaṃ paścājjñātiṣu saṃnamet | [KāSū, 3, 1 21.1]
na tv eva hīnasaṃbandhaṃ kuryāt sadbhir vininditam | [KāSū, 3, 1 21.2]
{KāSū, 3, 2}
saṃgatayostrirātram adhaḥśayyā brahmacaryaṃ kṣāralavaṇavarjam āhārastathā saptāhaṃ satūryamaṅgalasnānaṃ prasādhanaṃ sahabhojanaṃ ca prekṣā saṃbandhināṃ ca pūjanam | [KāSū, 3, 2 1.1]
iti sārvavarṇikam | [KāSū, 3, 2 1.2]
tasminn etāṃ niśi vijane mṛdubhir upacārair upakrameta | [KāSū, 3, 2 2.1]
trirātram avacanaṃ hi stambham iva nāyakaṃ paśyantī kanyā nirvidyeta paribhavecca tṛtīyām iva prakṛtim | [KāSū, 3, 2 3.1]
iti bābhravīyāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 3.2]
upakrameta viśrambhayecca na tu brahmacaryam ativarteta | [KāSū, 3, 2 4.1]
iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 4.2]
upakramamāṇaśca na prasahya kiṃcid ācaret | [KāSū, 3, 2 5.1]
kusumasadharmāṇo hi yoṣitaḥ sukumāropakramāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 6.1]
tāstvanadhigataviśvāsaiḥ prasabham upakramyamāṇāḥ saṃprayogadveṣiṇyo bhavanti | [KāSū, 3, 2 6.2]
tasmāt sāmnaivopacaret | [KāSū, 3, 2 6.3]
yuktyāpi tu yataḥ prasaram upalabhet tenaivānu praviśet | [KāSū, 3, 2 7.1]
tatpriyeṇāliṅganenācaritena | [KāSū, 3, 2 8.1]
nātikālatvāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 8.2]
pūrvakāyeṇa copakramet | [KāSū, 3, 2 9.1]
viṣahyatvāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 9.2]
dīpāloke vigāḍhayauvanāyāḥ pūrvasaṃstutāyāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 10.1]
bālāyā apūrvāyāścāndhakāre | [KāSū, 3, 2 10.2]
aṅgīkṛtapariṣvaṅgāyāśca vadanena tāmbūladānam | [KāSū, 3, 2 11.1]
tadapratipadyamānāṃ ca sāntvanair vākyaiḥ śapathaiḥ pratiyācitaiḥ pādapatanaiśca grāhayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 11.2]
vrīḍāyuktāpi yoṣidatyantakruddhāpi na pādapatanam ativartate iti sārvatrikam | [KāSū, 3, 2 11.3]
taddānaprasaṅgeṇa mṛdu viśadam akāhalam asyāścumbanam | [KāSū, 3, 2 12.1]
tatra siddhām ālāpayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 12.2]
tacchravaṇārthaṃ yat kiṃcid alpākṣarābhidheyam ajānann iva pṛcchet | [KāSū, 3, 2 12.3]
tatra niṣpratipattim anudvejayan sāntvanāyuktaṃ bahuśa eva pṛcchet | [KāSū, 3, 2 12.4]
tatra apyavadantīṃ nirbadhnīyāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 12.5]
sarvā eva hi kanyāḥ puruṣeṇa prayujyamānaṃ vacanaṃ viṣahante | [KāSū, 3, 2 13.1]
na tu laghumiśrām api vācaṃ vadanti | [KāSū, 3, 2 13.2]
iti ghoṭakamukhaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 13.3]
nirbadhyamānā tu śiraḥkampena prativacanāni yojayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 14.1]
kalahe tu na śiraḥ kampayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 14.2]
icchasi māṃ necchasi vā kiṃ te ahaṃ rucito na rucito veti pṛṣṭā ciraṃ sthitvā nirbadhyamānā tadānukūlyena śiraḥ kampayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 15.1]
prapañcyamānā tu vivadet | [KāSū, 3, 2 15.2]
saṃstutā cet sakhīm anukūlām ubhayato 'pi visrabdhāṃ tām antarā kṛtvā kathāṃ yojayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 16.1]
tasminn adhomukhī vihaset | [KāSū, 3, 2 16.2]
tāṃ cātivādinīm adhikṣiped vivadecca | [KāSū, 3, 2 16.3]
sā tu parihāsārtham idam anayoktam iti cānuktam api brūyāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 16.4]
tatra tām apanudya prativacanārtham abhyarthyamānā tūṣṇīm āsīta | [KāSū, 3, 2 16.5]

nāyakaṃ ca vihasantī kadācit kaṭākṣaiḥ prekṣeta | [KāSū, 3, 2 16.7]
ityālāpayojanam | [KāSū, 3, 2 16.8]
evaṃ jātaparicayā cānirvadantī tatsamīpe yācitaṃ tāmbūlaṃ vilepanaṃ srajaṃ nidadhyāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 17.1]
uttarīye vāsya nibadhnīyāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 17.2]
tathā yuktām ācchuritakena stanamukulayor upari spṛśet | [KāSū, 3, 2 17.3]
vāryamāṇaśca tvam api māṃ pariṣvajasva tato naivam ācariṣyāmīti sthityā pariṣvañjayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 17.4]
svaṃ ca hastam ā nābhideśāt prasārya nirvartayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 17.5]
krameṇa cainām utsaṅgam āropyādhikam adhikam upakramet | [KāSū, 3, 2 17.6]
apratipadyamānāṃ ca bhīṣayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 17.7]
ahaṃ khalu tava dantapadānyadhare kariṣyāmi stanapṛṣṭhe ca nakhapadam | [KāSū, 3, 2 18.1]
ātmanaśca svayaṃ kṛtvā tvayā kṛtam iti te sakhījanasya purataḥ kathayiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 3, 2 18.2]
sā tvaṃ kim atra vakṣyasīti bālavibhīṣikair bālapratyāyanaiśca śanair enāṃ pratārayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 18.3]
dvitīyasyāṃ tṛtīyasyāṃ ca rātrau kiṃcid adhikaṃ viśrambhitāṃ hastena yojayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 18.4]
sarvāṅgikaṃ cumbanam upakrameta | [KāSū, 3, 2 19.1]
ūrvoścopari vinyastahastaḥ saṃvāhanakriyāyāṃ siddhāyāṃ krameṇorumūlam api saṃvāhayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.1]
nivārite saṃvāhane ko doṣa ityākulayed enām | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.2]
tacca sthirīkuryāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.3]
tatra siddhāyā guhyadeśābhimarśanaṃ raśanāviyojanaṃ nīvīvisraṃsanaṃ vasanaparivartanam ūrumūlasaṃvāhanaṃ ca | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.4]
ete cāsyānyāpadeśāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.5]
yuktayantrāṃ rañjayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.6]
na tvakāle vratakhaṇḍanam anuśiṣyācca | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.7]
ātmānurāgaṃ darśayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.8]
manorathāṃśca pūrvakālikān anuvarṇayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.9]
āyatyāṃ ca tadānukūlyena pravṛttiṃ pratijānīyāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.10]
sapatnībhyaśca sādhvasam avacchindyāt | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.11]

iti kanyāvisrambhaṇam | [KāSū, 3, 2 20.13]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 21.1]
evaṃ cittānugo bālām upāyena prasādhayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 21.2]
tathāsya sānuraktā ca suvisrabdhā prajāyate | [KāSū, 3, 2 21.3]
nātyantam ānulomyena na cātiprātilomyataḥ | [KāSū, 3, 2 22.1]
siddhiṃ gacchati kanyāsu tasmān madhyena sādhayet | [KāSū, 3, 2 22.2]
ātmanaḥ prītijananaṃ yoṣitāṃ mānavardhanam | [KāSū, 3, 2 23.1]
kanyāvisrambhaṇaṃ vetti yaḥ sa tāsāṃ priyo bhavet | [KāSū, 3, 2 23.2]
atilajjānvitety eyaṃ yastu kanyām upekṣate | [KāSū, 3, 2 24.1]
so 'nabhiprāyavedīti paśuvat paribhūyate | [KāSū, 3, 2 24.2]
sahasā vāpyupakrāntā kanyācittam avindatā | [KāSū, 3, 2 25.1]

{KāSū, 3, 3}
dhanahīnastu guṇayukto 'pi madhyasthaguṇo hīnāpadeśo vā sadhano vā prātiveśyaḥ mātṛpitṛbhrātṛṣu ca paratantraḥ bālavṛttir ucitapraveśo vā kanyām alabhyatvān na varayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 1.1]
bālyāt prabhṛti caināṃ svayam evānurañjayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 1.2]
tathāyuktaśca mātulakulānuvartī dakṣiṇāpathe bāla eva mātrā ca pitrā ca viyuktaḥ paribhūtakalpo dhanotkarṣādalabhyāṃ mātuladuhitaram anyasmai vā pūrvadattāṃ sādhayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 1.3]
anyām api bāhyāṃ spṛhayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 1.4]
bālāyām evaṃ sati dharmādhigame saṃvananaṃ ślāghyam iti ghoṭakamukhaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 3 1.5]
tayā saha puṣpāvacayaṃ grathanaṃ gṛhakaṃ duhitṛkākrīḍāyojanaṃ bhaktapānakaraṇam iti kurvīta | [KāSū, 3, 3 2.1]
paricayasya vayasaścānurūpyāt | [KāSū, 3, 3 2.2]
ākarṣakrīḍā paṭṭikākrīḍā muṣṭidyūtakṣullakādidyūtāni madhyamāṅguligrahaṇaṃ ṣaṭpāṣāṇakādīni ca deśyāni tatsātmyāt tadāptadāsaceṭikābhis tayā ca sahānukrīḍeta | [KāSū, 3, 3 2.3]
kṣveḍitakāni sunimīlitakām ārabdhikāṃ lavaṇavīthikām anilatāḍitakāṃ godhūmapuñjikām aṅgulitāḍitakāṃ sakhībhir anyāni ca deśyāni | [KāSū, 3, 3 2.4]
yāṃ ca viśvāsyām asyāṃ manyeta tayā saha nirantarāṃ prītiṃ kuryāt | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.1]
paricayāṃśca budhyeta | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.2]
dhātreyikāṃ cāsyāḥ priyahitābhyām adhikam upagṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.3]
sā hi prīyamāṇā viditākārāpy apratyādiśantī taṃ tāṃ ca yojayituṃ śaknuyāt | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.4]
anabhihitāpi pratyācāryakam | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.5]
aviditākārāpi hi guṇān evānurāgāt prakāśayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.6]
yathā prayojyānurajyeta | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.7]
yatra yatra ca kautukaṃ prayojyāyāstad anu praviśya sādhayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.8]
krīḍanakadravyāṇi yānyapūrvāṇi yānyanyāsāṃ viralaśo vidyeraṃstānyasyā ayatnena sampādayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.9]
tatra kandukam anekabhakticitram alpakālāntaritam anyad anyacca saṃdarśayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.10]
tathā sūtradārugavalagajadantamayīr duhitṛkā madhūcchiṣṭapiṣṭamṛṇmayīśca | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.11]
bhaktapākārtham asyā mahānasikasya ca darśanam | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.12]
kāṣṭhamedhrakayośca saṃyuktayośca strīpuṃsayor ajaiḍakānāṃ devakulagṛhakānāṃ mṛdvidalakāṣṭhavinirmitānāṃ śukaparabhṛtamadanasārikālāvakakukkuṭatittiripañjarakāṇāṃ ca vicitrākṛtisaṃyuktānāṃ jalabhājanānāṃ ca yantrikāṇāṃ vīṇikānāṃ paṭolikānām alaktakamanaḥśilāharitālahiṅgulakaśyāmavarṇakādīnāṃ tathā candanakuṅkumayoḥ pūgaphalānāṃ pattrāṇāṃ kālayuktānāṃ ca śaktiviṣaye pracchannaṃ dānaṃ prakāśadravyāṇāṃ ca prakāśam | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.13]
yathā ca sarvābhiprāyasaṃvardhakam enaṃ manyeta tathā prayatitavyam | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.14]
vīkṣaṇe ca pracchannam arthayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.15]
tathā kathāyojanam | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.16]
pracchannadānasya tu kāraṇam ātmano gurujanād bhayaṃ khyāpayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.17]
deyasya cānyena spṛhaṇīyatvam iti | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.18]
vardhamānānurāgaṃ cākhyānake manaḥ kurvatīm anvarthābhiḥ kathābhiścittahāriṇībhiśca rañjayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.19]
vismayeṣu prasahyamānām indrajālaiḥ prayogair vismāpayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.20]
kalāsu kautukinīṃ tatkauśalena gītapriyāṃ śrutiharair gītaiḥ | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.21]
āśvayujyām aṣṭamīcandrake kaumudyām utsaveṣu yātrāyāṃ grahaṇe gṛhācāre vā vicitrair āpīḍaiḥ karṇapattrabhaṅgaiḥ sikthakapradhānair vastrāṅgulīyakabhūṣaṇadānaiśca | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.22]
no ced doṣakarāṇi manyeta | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.23]
anyapuruṣaviśeṣābhijñatayā dhātreyikāsyāḥ puruṣapravṛttau cātuḥṣaṣṭikān yogān grāhayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.24]
tadgrahaṇopadeśena ca prayojyāyāṃ ratikauśalam ātmanaḥ prakāśayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.25]
udāraveṣaśca svayam anupahatadarśanaḥ syāt | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.26]
bhāvaṃ ca kurvatīm iṅgitākāraiḥ sūcayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.27]
yuvatayo hi saṃsṛṣṭam abhīkṣṇadarśanaṃ ca puruṣaṃ prathamaṃ kāmayante | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.28]
kāmayamānā api tu nābhiyuñjata iti prāyovādaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.29]
iti bālāyām upakramāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 3 3.30]
tān iṅgitākārān vakṣyāmaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 3 4.1]
saṃmukhaṃ taṃ tu na vīkṣate | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.1]
vīkṣitā vrīḍāṃ darśayati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.2]
rucyam ātmano 'ṅgam apadeśena prakāśayati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.3]
pramattaṃ pracchannaṃ nāyakam atikrāntaṃ ca vīkṣate | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.4]
pṛṣṭā ca kiṃcit sasmitam avyaktākṣaram anavasitārthaṃ ca mandaṃ mandam adhomukhī kathayati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.5]
tatsamīpe ciraṃ sthānam abhinandati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.6]
dūre sthitā paśyatu mām iti manyamānā parijanaṃ savadanavikāram ābhāṣate | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.7]
taṃ deśaṃ na muñcati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.8]
yat kiṃcid dṛṣṭvā vihasitaṃ karoti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.9]
tatra kathām avasthānārtham anubadhnāti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.10]
bālasyāṅkagatasyāliṅganaṃ cumbanaṃ ca karoti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.11]
paricārikāyāstilakaṃ ca racayati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.12]
parijanānavaṣṭabhya tāstāśca līlā darśayati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.13]
tanmitreṣu viśvasiti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.14]
vacanaṃ caiṣāṃ bahu manyate karoti ca | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.15]
tatparicārakaiḥ saha prītiṃ saṃkathāṃ dyūtam iti ca karoti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.16]
svakarmasu ca prabhaviṣṇur ivaitān niyuṅkte | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.17]
teṣu ca nāyakasaṃkathām anyasya kathayatsvavahitā tāṃ śṛṇoti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.18]
dhātreyikayā coditā nāyakasyodavasitaṃ praviśati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.19]
tām antarā kṛtvā tena saha dyūtaṃ krīḍām ālāpaṃ cāyojayitum icchati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.20]
analaṃkṛtā darśanapathaṃ pariharati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.21]
karṇapattram aṅgulīyakaṃ srajaṃ vā tena yācitā sadhīram eva gātrād avatārya sakhyā haste dadāti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.22]
tena ca dattaṃ nityaṃ dhārayati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.23]
anyavarasaṃkathāsu viṣaṇṇā bhavati | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.24]
tatpakṣakaiśca saha na saṃsṛjyata iti | [KāSū, 3, 3 5.25]
bhavataścātra ślokau | [KāSū, 3, 3 6.1]
dṛṣṭvaitān bhāvasaṃyuktān ākārān iṅgitāni ca | [KāSū, 3, 3 6.2]
kanyāyāḥ saṃprayogārthaṃ tāṃstān yogān vicintayet | [KāSū, 3, 3 6.3]
bālakrīḍanakair bālā kalābhir yauvane sthitā | [KāSū, 3, 3 7.1]
vatsalā cāpi saṃgrāhyā viśvāsyajanasaṃgrahāt | [KāSū, 3, 3 7.2]
{KāSū, 3, 4}
darśiteṅgitākārāṃ kanyām upāyato 'bhiyuñjīta | [KāSū, 3, 4 1.1]
dyūte krīḍanakeṣu ca vivadamānaḥ sākāram asyāḥ pāṇim avalambeta | [KāSū, 3, 4 2.1]
yathoktaṃ ca spṛṣṭakādikam āliṅganavidhiṃ vidadhyāt | [KāSū, 3, 4 3.1]
patracchedyakriyāyāṃ ca svābhiprāyāsūcakaṃ mithunam asyā darśayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 4.1]
evam anyadviralaśo darśayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 5.1]
jalakrīḍāyāṃ taddūrato 'psu nimagnaḥ samīpam asyā gatvā spṛṣṭvā caināṃ tatraivonmajjet | [KāSū, 3, 4 6.1]
navapatrikādiṣu ca saviśeṣabhāvanivedanam | [KāSū, 3, 4 7.1]
ātmaduḥkhasyānirvedena kathanam | [KāSū, 3, 4 8.1]
svapnasya ca bhāvayuktasyānyāpadeśena | [KāSū, 3, 4 9.1]
prekṣaṇake svajanasamāje vā samīpopaveśanam | [KāSū, 3, 4 10.1]
tatrānyāpadiṣṭaṃ sparśanam | [KāSū, 3, 4 10.2]
apāśrayārthaṃ ca caraṇena caraṇasya pīḍanam | [KāSū, 3, 4 11.1]
tataḥ śanakair ekaikām aṅgulim abhispṛśet | [KāSū, 3, 4 12.1]
pādāṅguṣṭhena ca nakhāgrāṇi ghaṭṭayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 13.1]
tatra siddhaḥ padāt padam adhikam ākāṅkṣet | [KāSū, 3, 4 14.1]
kṣāntyarthaṃ ca tad evābhyaset | [KāSū, 3, 4 15.1]
pādaśauce pādāṅgulisaṃdaṃśena tadaṅgulipīḍanam | [KāSū, 3, 4 16.1]
dravyasya samarpaṇe pratigrahe vā tadgato vikāraḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 17.1]
ācamanānte codakenāsekaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 18.1]
vijane tamasi ca dvandvam āsīnaḥ kṣāntiṃ kurvīta | [KāSū, 3, 4 19.1]
samānadeśaśayyāyāṃ ca | [KāSū, 3, 4 19.2]
tatra yathārtham anudvejayato bhāvanivedanam | [KāSū, 3, 4 20.1]
vivikte ca kiṃcid asti kathayitavyam ityuktvā nirvacanaṃ bhāvaṃ ca tatropalakṣayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 21.1]
yathā pāradārike vakṣyāmaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 21.2]
viditabhāvastu vyādhim apadiśyaināṃ vārtāgrahaṇārthaṃ svam udavasitam ānayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 22.1]
āgatāyāśca śiraḥpīḍane niyogaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 23.1]
pāṇim avalambya cāsyāḥ sākāraṃ nayanayor lalāṭe ca nidadhyāt | [KāSū, 3, 4 23.2]
auṣadhāpadeśārthaṃ cāsyāḥ karma vinirdiśet | [KāSū, 3, 4 24.1]
idaṃ tvayā kartavyam | [KāSū, 3, 4 25.1]
na hyetad ṛte kanyayā anyena kāryam iti gacchantīṃ punar āgamanānubandham enāṃ visṛjet | [KāSū, 3, 4 25.2]
asya ca yogasya trirātraṃ trisaṃdhyaṃ ca prayuktiḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 26.1]
abhīkṣṇadarśanārtham āgatāyāśca goṣṭhīṃ vardhayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 27.1]
anyābhir api saha viśvāsanārtham adhikam adhikaṃ cābhiyuñjīta | [KāSū, 3, 4 28.1]
na tu vācā nirvadet | [KāSū, 3, 4 28.2]
dūragatabhāvo 'pi hi kanyāsu na nirvedena sidhyatīti ghoṭakamukhaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 29.1]
yadā tu bahusiddhāṃ manyeta tadaivopakramet | [KāSū, 3, 4 30.1]
pradoṣe niśi tamasi ca yoṣito mandasādhvasāḥ suratavyavasāyinyo rāgavatyaśca bhavanti | [KāSū, 3, 4 31.1]
na ca puruṣaṃ pratyācakṣate | [KāSū, 3, 4 31.2]
tasmāt tatkālaṃ prayojayitavyā iti prāyovādaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 31.3]
ekapuruṣābhiyogānāṃ tvasaṃbhave gṛhītārthayā dhātreyikayā sakhyā vā tasyām antarbhūtayā tam artham anirvadantyā sahainām aṅkam ānāyayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 32.1]
tato yathoktam abhiyuñjīta | [KāSū, 3, 4 32.2]
svāṃ vā paricārikām ādāv eva sakhītvenāsyāḥ praṇidadhyāt | [KāSū, 3, 4 33.1]
yajñe vivāhe yātrāyām utsave vyasane prekṣaṇakavyāpṛte jane tatra tatra ca dṛṣṭeṅgitākārāṃ parīkṣitabhāvām ekākinīm upakrameta | [KāSū, 3, 4 34.1]
na hi dṛṣṭabhāvā yoṣito deśe kāle ca prayujyamānā vyāvartanta iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 34.2]
ityekapuruṣābhiyogāḥ | [KāSū, 3, 4 34.3]
mandāpadeśā guṇavatyapi kanyā dhanahīnā kulīnāpi samānair ayācyāmānā mātāpitṛviyuktā vā jñātikulavartinī vā prāptayauvanā pāṇigrahaṇaṃ svayam abhīpseta | [KāSū, 3, 4 34.4]
sā tu guṇavantaṃ śaktaṃ sudarśanaṃ bālaprītyābhiyojayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 35.1]
yaṃ vā manyeta mātāpitror asamīkṣayā svayam apyayam indriyadaurbalyān mayi pravartiṣyata iti priyahitopacārair abhīkṣṇasaṃdarśanena ca tam āvarjayet | [KāSū, 3, 4 36.1]
mātā caināṃ sakhībhir dhātreyikābhiśca saha tadabhimukhīṃ kuryāt | [KāSū, 3, 4 37.1]

tataḥ śrotriyāgārād agnim iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [KāSū, 3, 5 5.2]
