{KāSū, 5, 2}
yathā kanyā svayam abhiyogasādhyā na tathā dūtyā | [KāSū, 5, 2 1.1]
parastriyastu sūkṣmabhāvā dūtīsādhyā na tathātmanetyācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 1.2]
sarvatra śaktiviṣaye svayaṃ sādhanam upapannatarakaṃ durupapādatvāt tasya dūtīprayoga iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 2.1]
prathamasāhasā aniyantraṇasaṃbhāṣāśca svayaṃ pratāryāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 3.1]
tadviparītāśca dūtyeti prāyovādaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 3.2]
svayam abhiyokṣyamāṇastv ādāv eva paricayaṃ kuryāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 4.1]
tasyāḥ svābhāvikaṃ darśanaṃ prāyatnikaṃ ca | [KāSū, 5, 2 5.1]
svābhāvikam ātmano bhavanasaṃnikarṣe prāyatnikaṃ mitrajñātimahāmātravaidyabhavanasaṃnikarṣe vivāhayajñotsavavyasanodyānagamanādiṣu | [KāSū, 5, 2 5.2]
darśane cāsyāḥ satataṃ sākāraṃ prekṣaṇaṃ keśasaṃyamanaṃ nakhāchuraṇam ābharaṇaprahlādanam adharaoṣṭhavimardanaṃ tāstāśca līlā vayasyaiḥ saha prekṣamāṇāyās tatsambaddhāḥ parāpadeśinyaśca kathāstyāgopabhogaprakāśanaṃ sakhyur utsaṅganiṣaṇṇasya sāṅgabhaṅgaṃ jṛmbhaṇam ekabhrūkṣepaṇaṃ mandavākyatā tadvākyaśravaṇaṃ tām uddiśya bālenānyajanena vā sahānyopadiṣṭā dvyarthā kathā tasyāṃ svayaṃ manorathāvedanam anyāpadeśena tām evoddiśya bālacumbanam āliṅganaṃ ca jihvayā cāsya tāmbūladānaṃ pradeśinyā hanudeśaghaṭṭanaṃ tat tad yathāyogaṃ yathāvakāśaṃ ca prayoktavyam | [KāSū, 5, 2 6.1]
tasyāścāṅkagatasya bālasya lālanaṃ bālakrīḍanakānāṃ cāsya dānaṃ grahaṇaṃ tena saṃnikṛṣṭatvāt kathāyojanaṃ tatsaṃbhāṣaṇakṣameṇa janena ca prītim āsādya kāryaṃ tadanubandhaṃ ca gamanāgamanasya yojanaṃ saṃśraye cāsyāstām apaśyato nāma kāmasūtrasaṃkathā | [KāSū, 5, 2 6.2]
prasṛte tu paricaye tasyā haste nyāsaṃ nikṣepaṃ ca nidadhyāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.1]
tatpratidinaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ caikadeśato gṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.2]
saugandhikaṃ pūgaphalāni ca | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.3]
tām ātmano dāraiḥ saha visrambhagoṣṭhyāṃ viviktāsane ca yojayet nityadarśanārthaṃ viśvāsanārthaṃ ca | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.4]
suvarṇakāramaṇikāravaikaṭikanīlīkusumbharañjakādiṣu ca kāmārthinyāṃ sahātmano vaśyaiścaiṣāṃ tatsaṃpādane svayaṃ prayateta | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.5]
tadanuṣṭhānaniratasya lokavidito dīrghakālaṃ saṃdarśanayogaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.6]
tasmiṃścānyeṣām api karmaṇām anusaṃdhānam | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.7]
yena karmaṇā dravyeṇa kauśalena cārthinī syāt tasya prayogam utpattim āgamam upāyaṃ vijñānaṃ cātmāyattaṃ darśayet | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.8]
pūrvapravṛtteṣu lokacariteṣu dravyaguṇaparīkṣāsu ca tayā tatparijanena ca saha vivādaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.9]
tatra nirdiṣṭāni paṇitāni teṣv enāṃ prāśnikatvena yojayet | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.10]
tayā tu vivadamāno 'tyantādbhutam iti brūyād iti paricayakāraṇāni | [KāSū, 5, 2 7.11]
kṛtaparicayāṃ darśiteṅgitākārāṃ kanyām ivopāyato 'bhiyuñjīteti | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.1]
prāyeṇa tatra sūkṣmā abhiyogāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.2]
kanyānām asaṃprayuktatvāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.3]
itarāsu tān eva sphuṭam upadadhyāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.4]
samprayuktatvāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.5]
saṃdarśitākārāyāṃ nirbhinnasadbhāvāyāṃ samupabhogavyatikare tadīyānyupayuñjīta | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.6]
tatra mahārhagandham uttarīyaṃ kusumaṃ ca ātmīyaṃ syād aṅgulīyakaṃ ca | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.7]
taddhastād gṛhītatāmbūlayā goṣṭhīgamanodyatasya keśahastapuṣpayācanam | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.8]
tatra mahārhagandhaṃ spṛhaṇīyaṃ svanakhadaśanapadacihnitaṃ sākāraṃ dadyāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.9]
adhikair adhikaiścābhiyogaiḥ sādhvasavicchedanam | [KāSū, 5, 2 8.10]
krameṇa ca viviktadeśe gamanam āliṅganaṃ cumbanaṃ tāmbūlasya grāhaṇaṃ dānānte dravyāṇāṃ parivartanaṃ guhyadeśābhimarśanaṃ cetyabhiyogāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 9.1]
yatra caikābhiyuktā na tatrāparām abhiyuñjīta | [KāSū, 5, 2 10.1]
tatra yā vṛddhānubhūtaviṣayā priyopagrahaiśca tām upagṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 5, 2 10.2]
ślokāvatra bhavataḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 11.1]
anyatra dṛṣṭasaṃcārastadbhartā yatra nāyakaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 11.2]
na tatra yoṣitaṃ kāṃcit suprāpām api laṅghayet | [KāSū, 5, 2 11.3]
śaṅkitāṃ rakṣitāṃ bhītāṃ saśvaśrūkāṃ ca yoṣitam | [KāSū, 5, 2 12.1]
na tarkayeta medhāvī jānan pratyayam ātmanaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 2 13.1]
{KāSū, 5, 3}
abhiyuñjāno yoṣitaḥ pravṛttiṃ parīkṣeta | [KāSū, 5, 3 1.1]
tayā bhāvaḥ parīkṣito bhavati | [KāSū, 5, 3 1.2]
abhiyogāṃśca pratigṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 5, 3 1.3]
mantram avṛṇvānāṃ dūtyaināṃ sādhayet | [KāSū, 5, 3 2.1]
apratigṛhyābhiyogaṃ punar api saṃsṛjyamānāṃ dvidhā bhūtamānasāṃ vidyāt | [KāSū, 5, 3 3.1]
tāṃ krameṇa sādhayet | [KāSū, 5, 3 3.2]
apratigṛhyābhiyogaṃ saviśeṣam alaṃkṛtā ca punar dṛśyeta tathaiva tam abhigacchecca vivikte balād grahaṇīyāṃ vidyāt | [KāSū, 5, 3 4.1]
bahūn api viṣahate abhiyogān na ca cireṇāpi prayacchatyātmānaṃ sā śuṣkapratigrāhiṇī paricayavighaṭanasādhyā | [KāSū, 5, 3 5.1]
manuṣyajāteścittānityatvāt | [KāSū, 5, 3 6.1]
abhiyuktāpi pariharati | [KāSū, 5, 3 7.1]
na ca saṃsṛjyate | [KāSū, 5, 3 7.2]
na ca pratyācaṣṭe | [KāSū, 5, 3 7.3]
tasminn ātmani ca gauravābhimānāt | [KāSū, 5, 3 7.4]
sātiparicayāt kṛcchrasādhyā | [KāSū, 5, 3 7.5]
marmajñayā dūtyā tāṃ sādhayet | [KāSū, 5, 3 7.6]
sā ced abhiyujyamānā pāruṣyeṇa pratyādiśatyupekṣyā | [KāSū, 5, 3 8.1]
paruṣayitvāpi tu prītiyojinīṃ sādhayet | [KāSū, 5, 3 9.1]
kāraṇāt saṃsparśanaṃ sahate nāvabudhyate nāma dvidhābhūtamānasā sātatyena kṣāntyā vā sādhyā | [KāSū, 5, 3 10.1]
samīpe śayānāyāḥ supto nāma karam upari vinyaset | [KāSū, 5, 3 10.2]
sāpi suptevopekṣate | [KāSū, 5, 3 10.3]
jāgratī tvapanuded bhūyo 'bhiyogākāṅkṣiṇī | [KāSū, 5, 3 10.4]
etena pādasyopari pādanyāso vyākhyātaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 3 11.1]
tasmin prasṛte bhūyaḥ suptasaṃśleṣaṇam upakramet | [KāSū, 5, 3 11.2]
tadasahamānām utthitāṃ dvitīye ahani prakṛtivartinīm abhiyogārthinīṃ vidyāt | [KāSū, 5, 3 11.3]
adṛśyamānāṃ tu dūtīsādhyām | [KāSū, 5, 3 11.4]
ciram adṛṣṭāpi prakṛtisthaiva saṃsṛjyate kṛtalakṣaṇāṃ tāṃ darśitākārām upakramet | [KāSū, 5, 3 12.1]
anabhiyuktāpyākārayati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.1]
vivikte cātmānaṃ darśayati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.2]
savepathugadgadaṃ vadati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.3]
svinnakaracaraṇāṅguliḥ svinnamukhī ca bhavati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.4]
śiraḥpīḍane saṃvāhane corvor ātmānaṃ nāyake niyojayati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.5]
āturā saṃvāhikā caikena hastena saṃvāhayantī dvitīyena bāhunā sparśam āvedayati śleṣayati ca | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.6]
vismitabhāvā | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.7]
nidrāndhā vā parispṛśyorubhyāṃ bāhubhyām api tiṣṭhati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.8]
alikaikadeśam ūrvor upari pātayati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.9]
ūrūmūlasaṃvāhane niyuktā na pratilomayati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.10]
tatraiva hastam ekam avicalaṃ nyasyati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.11]
aṅgasaṃdaṃśena ca pīḍitaṃ cirād apanayati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.12]
pratigṛhyaivaṃ nāyakābhiyogān punar dvitīye ahani saṃvāhanāyopagacchati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.13]
nātyarthaṃ saṃsṛjyate | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.14]
na ca pariharati | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.15]
vivikte bhāvaṃ darśayati niṣkāraṇaṃ cāgūḍham anyatra pracchannapradeśāt | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.16]
saṃnikṛṣṭaparicārakopabhogyā sā ced ākāritāpi tathaiva syāt sā marmajñayā dūtyā sādhyā | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.17]
vyāvartamānā tu tarkaṇīyeti bhāvaparīkṣā | [KāSū, 5, 3 13.18]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 3 14.1]
ādau paricayaṃ kuryāt tataśca paribhāṣaṇam | [KāSū, 5, 3 14.2]
paribhāṣaṇasaṃmiśraṃ mithaścākāravedanam | [KāSū, 5, 3 14.3]
pratyuttareṇa paśyecced ākārasya parigraham | [KāSū, 5, 3 15.1]
tato 'bhiyuñjīta naraḥ striyaṃ vigatasādhvasaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 3 15.2]
ākāreṇātmano bhāvaṃ yā nārī prāk prayojayet | [KāSū, 5, 3 16.1]
kṣipram evābhiyojyā sā prathame tv eva darśane | [KāSū, 5, 3 16.2]
ślakṣṇam ākāritā yā tu darśayet sphuṭam uttaram | [KāSū, 5, 3 17.1]
sāpi tatkṣaṇasiddheti vijñeyā ratilālasā | [KāSū, 5, 3 17.2]
dhīrāyām apragalbhāyāṃ parīkṣiṇyāṃ ca yoṣiti | [KāSū, 5, 3 18.1]
eṣa sūkṣmo vidhiḥ proktaḥ siddhā eva sphuṭaṃ striyaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 3 18.2]
{KāSū, 5, 4}
darśiteṅgitākārāṃ tu praviraladarśanām apūrvāṃ ca dūtyopasarpayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.1]
saināṃ śīlato 'nupraviśyākhyānakapaṭaiḥ subhagaṃkaraṇayogair lokavṛttāntaiḥ kavikathābhiḥ pāradārikakathābhiśca tasyāśca rūpavijñānadākṣiṇyaśīlānupraśaṃsābhiśca tāṃ rañjayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.2]
katham evaṃvidhāyāstavāyam itthaṃbhūtaḥ patiriti cānuśayaṃ grāhayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.3]
na tava subhage dāsyam api kartuṃ yukta iti brūyāt | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.4]
mandavegatām īrṣyālutāṃ śaṭhatām akṛtajñatāṃ cāsaṃbhogaśīlatāṃ kadaryatāṃ capalatām anyāni ca yāni tasmin guptānyasyā abhyāśe sati sadbhāve atiśayena bhāṣeta | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.5]
yena ca doṣeṇodvignāṃ lakṣayet tenaivānupraviśet | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.6]
yadāsau mṛgī tadā naiva śaśatādoṣaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.7]
etenaiva vaḍavāhastinīviṣayaścoktaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 1.8]
nāyikāyā eva tu viśvāsyatām upalabhya dūtītvenopasarpayet prathamasāhasāyāṃ sūkṣmabhāvāyāṃ ceti goṇikāputraḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 2.1]
sā nāyakasya caritam anulomatāṃ kāmitāni ca kathayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.1]
prasṛtasadbhāvāyāṃ ca yuktyā kāryaśarīram itthaṃ vadet | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.2]
śṛṇu vicitram idaṃ subhage tvāṃ kila dṛṣṭvāmutrāsāv itthaṃ gotraputro nāyakaścittonmādam anubhavati | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.3]
prakṛtyā sukumāraḥ kadācid anyatrāparikliṣṭapūrvastapasvī | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.4]
tato 'dhunā śakyam anena maraṇam apyanubhavitum iti varṇayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.5]
tatra siddhā dvitīye ahani vāci vaktre dṛṣṭyāṃ ca prasādam upalakṣya punar api kathāṃ pravartayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.6]
śṛṇvatyāṃ cāhalyāvimārakaśākuntalādīny anyānyapi laukikāni ca kathayet tadyuktāni | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.7]
vṛṣatāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭivijñatāṃ saubhāgyaṃ ca nāyakasya | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.8]
ślāghanīyatāṃ cāsya pracchannaṃ saṃprayogaṃ bhūtam abhūtapūrvaṃ vā varṇayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.9]
ākāraṃ cāsyā lakṣayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 3.10]
savihasitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sambhāṣate | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.1]
āsane copanimantrayate | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.2]
kvāsitaṃ kva śayitaṃ kva bhuktaṃ kva ceṣṭitaṃ kiṃ vā kṛtam iti pṛcchati | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.3]
vivikte darśayatyātmānam | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.4]
ākhyānakāni niyuṅkte | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.5]
cintayantī niḥśvasiti vijṛmbhate ca | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.6]
prītidāyaṃ ca dadāti | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.7]
iṣṭeṣūtsaveṣu ca smarati | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.8]
punar darśanānubandhaṃ visṛjati | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.9]
sādhuvādinī satī kim idam aśobhanam abhidhatsa iti kathām anubadhnāti | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.10]
nāyakasya śāṭhyacāpalyasambaddhān doṣān dadāti | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.11]
pūrvapravṛttaṃ ca tatsaṃdarśanaṃ kathābhiyogaṃ ca svayam akathayantī tayocyamānam ākāṅkṣati | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.12]
nāyakamanoratheṣu ca kathyamāneṣu saparibhavaṃ nāma hasati | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.13]
na ca nirvadatīti | [KāSū, 5, 4 4.14]
dūtyenāṃ darśitākārāṃ nāyakābhijñānair upabṛṃhayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 5.1]
asaṃstutāṃ tu guṇakathanair anurāgakathābhiścāvarjayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 5.2]
nāsaṃstutādṛṣṭākārayor dūtyam astītyauddālakiḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 6.1]
asaṃstutayor api saṃsṛṣṭākārayor astīti bābhravīyāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 6.2]
saṃstutayor apyasaṃsṛṣṭākārayor astīti goṇikāputraḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 6.3]
asaṃstutayor adṛṣṭākārayor api dūtīpratyayād iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 6.4]
tāsāṃ manoharāṇyupāyanāni tāmbūlam anulepanaṃ srajam aṅgulīyakaṃ vāso vā tena prahitaṃ darśayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 7.1]
teṣu nāyakasya yathārthaṃ nakhadaśanapadāni tāni tāni ca cihnāni syuḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 7.2]
vāsasi ca kuṅkumāṅkam añjaliṃ nidadhyāt | [KāSū, 5, 4 7.3]
pattrachedyāni nānābhiprāyākṛtini darśayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 7.4]
lekhapatragarbhāṇi karṇapattrāṇyāpīḍāṃśca teṣu svamanorathākhyāpanam | [KāSū, 5, 4 7.5]
pratiprābhṛtadāne caināṃ niyojayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 7.6]
evaṃ kṛtaparasparaparigrahayośca dūtīpratyayaḥ samāgamaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 7.7]
sa tu devatābhigamane yātrāyām udyānakrīḍāyāṃ jalāvataraṇe vivāhe yajñavyasanotsaveṣv agnyutpāte cauravibhrame janapadasya cakrārohaṇe prekṣāvyāpāreṣu teṣu teṣu ca kāryeṣv iti bābhravīyāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 8.1]
sakhībhikṣukīkṣapaṇikātāpasībhavaneṣu sukhopāya iti goṇikāputraḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 8.2]
tasyā eva tu gehe viditaniṣkramapraveśe cintitātyayapratīkāre praveśanam upapannaṃ niṣkramaṇam avijñātakālaṃ ca tan nityaṃ sukhopāyaṃ ceti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 8.3]
nisṛṣṭārthā parimitārthā patrahārī svayaṃdūtī mūḍhadūtī bhāryādūtī mūkadūtī vātadūtī ceti dūtīviśeṣāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 9.1]
nāyakasya nāyikāyāśca yathāmanīṣitam artham upalabhya svabuddhyā kāryasaṃpādinī nisṛṣṭārthā | [KāSū, 5, 4 10.1]
sā prāyeṇa saṃstutasaṃbhāṣaṇayoḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 11.1]
nāyikayā prayuktāsaṃstutasaṃbhāṣaṇayor api | [KāSū, 5, 4 11.2]
kautukāccānurūpau yuktāv imau parasparasyetyasaṃstutayor api | [KāSū, 5, 4 11.3]
kāryaikadeśam abhiyogaikadeśaṃ copalabhya śeṣaṃ sampādayatīti parimitārthā | [KāSū, 5, 4 12.1]
sā dṛṣṭaparasparākārayoḥ praviraladarśanayoḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 13.1]
saṃdeśamātraṃ prāpayatīti patrahārī | [KāSū, 5, 4 14.1]
sā pragāḍhasadbhāvayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayośca deśakālasaṃbodhanārtham | [KāSū, 5, 4 15.1]
dautyena prahitānyayā svayam eva nāyakam abhigacched ajānatī nāma tena sahopabhogaṃ svapne vā kathayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.1]
gotraskhalitaṃ bhāryāṃ cāsya nindet | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.2]
tadvyapadeśena svayam īrṣyāṃ darśayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.3]
nakhadaśanacihnitaṃ vā kiṃcid dadyāt | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.4]
bhavate aham adau dātuṃ saṃkalpiteti cābhidadhīta | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.5]
mama bhāryāyā kā ramanīyeti vivikte paryanuyuñjīta sā svayaṃdūtī | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.6]
tasyā vivikte darśanaṃ pratigrahaśca | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.7]
pratigrahacchalenānyām abhisaṃdhāyāsyāḥ saṃdeśaśrāvaṇadvāreṇa nāyakaṃ sādhayet tāṃ copahanyāt sāpi svayaṃdūtī | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.8]
etayā nāyako 'pyanyadūtaśca vyākhyātaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 16.9]
nāyakabhāryāṃ mugdhāṃ viśvāsyāyantraṇayānupraviśya nāyakasya ceṣṭitāni pṛcchet | [KāSū, 5, 4 17.1]
yogāñ śikṣayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 17.2]
sākāraṃ maṇḍayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 17.3]
kopam enāṃ grāhayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 17.4]
evaṃ ca pratipadyasveti śrāvayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 17.5]
svayaṃ cāsyāṃ nakhadaśanapadāni nirvartayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 17.6]
tena dvāreṇa nāyakam ākārayet sā mūḍhadūtī | [KāSū, 5, 4 17.7]
tasyāstayaiva pratyuttarāṇi yojayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 18.1]
svabhāryāṃ vā mūḍhāṃ prayojya tayā saha viśvāsena yojayitvā tayaivākārayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 19.1]
ātmanaśca vaicakṣaṇyaṃ prakāśayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 19.2]
sā bhāryādūtī | [KāSū, 5, 4 19.3]
tasyāstayaivākāragrahaṇam | [KāSū, 5, 4 19.4]
bālāṃ vā paricārikām adoṣajñām aduṣṭenopāyena prahiṇuyāt | [KāSū, 5, 4 20.1]
tatra sraji karṇapattre vā gūḍhalekhanidhānaṃ nakhadaśanapadaṃ vā sā mūkadūtī | [KāSū, 5, 4 20.2]
tasyāstayā eva pratyuttaraprārthanam | [KāSū, 5, 4 20.3]
pūrvaprastutārthaliṅgasambaddham anyajanāgrahaṇīyaṃ laukikārthaṃ dvyarthaṃ vā vacanam udāsīnā yā śrāvayet sā vātadūtī | [KāSū, 5, 4 21.1]
tasyā api tayaiva pratyuttaraprārthanam iti tāsāṃ viśeṣāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 21.2]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 4 22.1]
vidhavekṣaṇikā dāsī bhikṣukī śilpakārikā | [KāSū, 5, 4 22.2]
praviśatyāśu viśvāsaṃ dūtīkāryaṃ ca vindati | [KāSū, 5, 4 22.3]
vidveṣaṃ grāhayet patyau ramaṇīyāni varṇayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 23.1]
citrān suratasaṃbhogān anyāsām api darśayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 23.2]
nāyakasyānurāgaṃ ca punaśca ratikauśalam | [KāSū, 5, 4 24.1]
prārthanāṃ cādhikastrībhir avaṣṭambhaṃ ca varṇayet | [KāSū, 5, 4 24.2]
asaṃkalpitam apyartham utsṛṣṭaṃ doṣakāraṇāt | [KāSū, 5, 4 25.1]
punar āvartayatyeva dūtī vacanakauśalāt | [KāSū, 5, 4 25.2]
{KāSū, 5, 5}
na rājñāṃ mahāmātrāṇāṃ vā parabhavanapraveśo vidyate | [KāSū, 5, 5 1.1]
mahājanena hi caritam eṣāṃ dṛśyate anuvidhīyate ca | [KāSū, 5, 5 1.2]
savitāram udyantaṃ trayo lokāḥ paśyanti anūdyante ca | [KāSū, 5, 5 2.1]
gacchantam api paśyanty anupratiṣṭhante ca | [KāSū, 5, 5 2.2]
tasmād aśakyatvād garhaṇīyatvācceti na te vṛthā kiṃcid ācareyuḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 3.1]
avaśyaṃ tv ācaritavye yogān prayuñjīran | [KāSū, 5, 5 4.1]
grāmādhipater ayuktakasya halotthavṛttiputrasya yūno grāmīṇayoṣito vacanamātrasādhyāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 5.1]
tāścarṣaṇya ityācakṣate viṭāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 5.2]
tābhiḥ saha viṣṭikarmasu koṣṭhāgārapraveśe dravyāṇāṃ niṣkramaṇapraveśanayor bhavanapratisaṃskāre kṣetrakarmaṇi karpāsorṇātasīśaṇavalkalādāne sūtrapratigrahe dravyāṇāṃ krayavikrayavinimayeṣu teṣu teṣu ca karmasu saṃprayogaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 6.1]
tathā vrajayoṣidbhiḥ saha gavādhyakṣasya | [KāSū, 5, 5 7.1]
vidhavānāthāpravrajitābhiḥ saha sūtrādhyakṣasya | [KāSū, 5, 5 8.1]
marmajñatvād rātrāvaṭane cāṭantībhir nāgarasya | [KāSū, 5, 5 9.1]
krayavikraye paṇyādhyakṣasya | [KāSū, 5, 5 10.1]
aṣṭamīcandrakaumudīsuvasantakādiṣu pattananagarakharvaṭayoṣitām īśvarabhavane saha antaḥpurikābhiḥ prāyeṇa krīḍā | [KāSū, 5, 5 11.1]
tatra cāpānakānte nagarastriyo yathāparicayam antaḥpurikāṇāṃ pṛthak pṛthag bhogāvāsakān praviśya kathābhir āsitvā pūjitāḥ prapītāścopapradoṣaṃ niṣkrāmayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 12.1]
tatra praṇihitā rājadāsī prayojyāyāḥ pūrvasaṃsṛṣṭā tāṃ tatra sambhāṣeta | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.1]
rāmaṇīyakadarśanena yojayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.2]
prāg eva svabhavanasthāṃ brūyāt | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.3]
amuṣyāṃ krīḍāyāṃ tava rājabhavanasthānāni rāmaṇīyakāni darśayiṣyāmīti kāle ca yojayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.4]
bahiḥ pravālakuṭṭimaṃ te darśayiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.5]
maṇibhūmikāṃ vṛkṣavāṭikāṃ mṛdvīkāmaṇḍapaṃ samudragṛhaprāsādān gūḍhabhittisaṃcārāṃścitrakarmāṇi krīḍāmṛgān yantrāṇi śakunān vyāghrasiṃhapañjarādīni ca yāni purastād varṇitāni syuḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.6]
ekānte ca tadgatam īśvarānurāgaṃ śrāvayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.7]
saṃprayoge cāturyaṃ cābhivarṇayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.8]
amantraśrāvaṃ ca pratipannāṃ yojayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 13.9]
apratipadyamānāṃ svayam eveśvara āgatyopacāraiḥ sānvitāṃ rañjayitvā sambhūya ca sānurāgaṃ visṛjet | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.1]
prayojyāyāśca patyur anugrahocitasya dārān nityam antaḥpuram aucityāt praveśayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.2]
tatra praṇihitā rājadāsīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.3]
antaḥpurikā vā prayojyayā saha svaceṭikā saṃpreṣaṇena prītiṃ kuryāt | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.4]
prasṛtaprītiṃ ca sāpadeśaṃ darśane niyojayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.5]
praviṣṭāṃ pūjitāṃ pītavartīm praṇihitā rājadāsīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.6]
yasmin vā vijñāne prayojyā vikhyātā syāt taddarśanārtham antaḥpurikā sopacāraṃ tām āhvayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.7]
praviṣṭāṃ praṇihitā rājadāsīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.8]
udbhūtānarthasya bhītasya vā bhāryāṃ bhikṣukī brūyāt asāvantaḥpurikā rājani siddhā gṛhītavākyā mama vacanaṃ śṛṇoti | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.9]
svabhāvataśca kṛpāśīlā tām anenopāyenādhigamiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.10]
aham eva te praveśaṃ kārayiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.11]
sā ca te bhartur mahāntam anarthaṃ nivartayiṣyatīti pratipannāṃ dvistrir iti praveśayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.12]
antaḥpurikā cāsyā abhayaṃ dadyāt | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.13]
abhayaśravaṇācca samprahṛṣṭāṃ praṇihitā rājadāsīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.14]
etayā vṛttyarthināṃ mahāmātrābhitaptānāṃ balād vigṛhītānāṃ vyavahāre durbalānāṃ svabhogenāsaṃtuṣṭānāṃ rājani prītikāmānāṃ rājyajaneṣu paṅktim icchatāṃ sajātair bādhyamānānāṃ sajātān bādhitukāmānāṃ sūcakānām anyeṣāṃ kāryavaśināṃ jāyā vyākhyātāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 14.15]
anyena vā prayojyāṃ saha saṃsṛṣṭāṃ saṃgrāhya dāsyam upanītāṃ krameṇāntaḥpuraṃ praveśayet | [KāSū, 5, 5 15.1]
praṇidhinā cāyatim asyāḥ saṃdūṣya rājani vidviṣṭa iti kalatrāvagrahopāyenainām antaḥpuraṃ praveśayed iti pracchannayogāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 15.2]
ete rājaputreṣu prāyeṇa | [KāSū, 5, 5 15.3]
na tv evaṃ parabhavanam īśvaraḥ praviśet | [KāSū, 5, 5 16.1]
ābhīraṃ hi koṭṭarājaṃ parabhavanagataṃ bhrātṛprayukto rajako jaghāna | [KāSū, 5, 5 17.1]
kāśirājaṃ jayasenam aśvādhyakṣa iti | [KāSū, 5, 5 17.2]
prakāśakāmitāni tu deśapravṛttiyogāt | [KāSū, 5, 5 18.1]
prattā janapadakanyā daśame ahani kiṃcid aupāyanikam upagṛhya praviśantyantaḥpuram upabhuktā eva visṛjyanta ityāndhrāṇām | [KāSū, 5, 5 19.1]
mahāmātreṣvarāṇām antaḥpurāṇi niśi sevārthaṃ rājānam upagacchanti vātsagulmakānām | [KāSū, 5, 5 19.2]
rūpavatīr janapadayoṣitaḥ prītyapadeśena māsaṃ māsārdhaṃ vātivāsayanty antaḥpurikā vaidarbhāṇām | [KāSū, 5, 5 19.3]
darśanīyāḥ svabhāryāḥ prītidāyām eva mahāmātrarājabhyo dadaty aparāntakānām | [KāSū, 5, 5 19.4]
rājakrīḍārthaṃ nagarastriyo janapadastriyaśca saṃghaśa ekaśaśca rājakulaṃ praviśanti saurāṣṭrakāṇām iti | [KāSū, 5, 5 19.5]
ślokāvatra bhavataḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 20.1]
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ prayogāḥ pāradārikāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 20.2]
deśe deśe pravartante rājabhiḥ sampravartitāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 20.3]
na tv evaitān prayuñjīta rājā lokahite rataḥ | [KāSū, 5, 5 21.1]
nigṛhītāriṣaḍvargastathā vijayate mahīm | [KāSū, 5, 5 21.2]
{KāSū, 5, 6}
nāntaḥpurāṇāṃ rakṣaṇayogāt puruṣasaṃdarśanaṃ vidyate patyuścaikatvād anekasādhāraṇatvāccātṛptiḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 1.1]
tasmāt tāni prayogata eva parasparaṃ rañjayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 1.2]
dhātreyikāṃ sakhīṃ dāsīṃ vā puruṣavad alaṃkṛtyākṛtisaṃyuktaiḥ kandamūlaphalāvayavair apadravyair vātmābhiprāyāṃ nirvartayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 2.1]
puruṣapratimā avyaktaliṅgāścādhiśayīran | [KāSū, 5, 6 3.1]
rājānaśca kṛpāśīlā vināpi bhāvayogād āyojitāpadravyā yāvadartham ekayā rātryā bahvībhir api gacchanti | [KāSū, 5, 6 4.1]
yasyāṃ tu prītir vāsaka ṛtuv vā tatrābhiprāyataḥ pravartanta iti prācyopacārāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 4.2]
strīyogeṇaiva puruṣāṇām apyalabdhavṛttīnāṃ viyoniṣu vijātiṣu strīpratimāsu kevalopamardanāccābhiprāyanivṛttir vyākhyātā | [KāSū, 5, 6 5.1]
yoṣaveṣāṃśca nāgarakān prāyeṇa antaḥpurikāḥ paricārikābhiḥ saha praveśayanti | [KāSū, 5, 6 6.1]
teṣām upāvartane dhātreyikāśca abhyantarasaṃsṛṣṭā āyatiṃ darśayantyaḥ prayateran | [KāSū, 5, 6 6.2]
sukhapraveśitām apasārabhūmiṃ viśālatāṃ veśmanaḥ pramādaṃ rakṣiṇām anityatāṃ parijanasya varṇayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 6.3]
na cāsadbhūtenārthena praveśayituṃ janam āvartayeyur doṣāt | [KāSū, 5, 6 6.4]
nāgarakastu suprāpam apyantaḥpuram apāyabhūyiṣṭhatvān na praviśed iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 7.1]
sāpasāraṃ tu pramadavanāvagāḍhaṃ vibhaktadīrghakakṣyam alpapramattarakṣakaṃ proṣitārājakaṃ kāraṇāni samīkṣya bahuśa āhūyamāno 'rthabuddhyā kakṣyāpraveśaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tābhir eva vihitopāyaḥ praviśet | [KāSū, 5, 6 8.1]
śaktiviṣaye ca pratidinaṃ niṣkrāmet | [KāSū, 5, 6 8.2]
bahiśca rakṣibhir anyad eva kāraṇam apadiśya saṃsṛjyeta | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.1]
antaścāriṇyāṃ ca paricārikāyāṃ viditārthāyāṃ saktam ātmānaṃ rūpayet | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.2]
tadalābhācca śokam antaḥpraveśinībhiśca dūtīkalpaṃ sakalam ācaret | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.3]
rājapraṇidhīṃśca budhyeta | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.4]
dūtyāstvasaṃcāre yatra gṛhītākārāyāḥ prayojyāyā darśanayogastatrāvasthānam | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.5]
tasminn api tu rakṣiṣu paricārikāvyapadeśaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.6]
cakṣuranubadhnatyām iṅgitākāranivedanam | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.7]
yatra saṃpāto 'syāstatra citrakarmaṇastad yuktasya vyarthānāṃ gītavastukānāṃ krīḍanakānāṃ kṛtacihnānām āpīnakānām aṅgulīyakasya ca nidhānam | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.8]
pratyuttaraṃ tayā dattaṃ prapaśyet | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.9]
tataḥ praveśane yateta | [KāSū, 5, 6 9.10]
yatra cāsyā niyataṃ gamanam iti vidyāt tatra pracchannasya prāg evāvasthānam | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.1]
rakṣipuruṣarūpo vā tadanujñātavelāyāṃ praviśet | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.2]
āstaraṇaprāvaraṇaveṣṭitasya vā praveśanirhārau | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.3]
puṭāpuṭayogair vā naṣṭacchāyārūpaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.4]
tatrāyaṃ prayogaḥ nakulahṛdayaṃ corakatumbīphalāni sarpākṣīṇi cāntardhūmena pacet | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.5]
tato 'ñjanena samabhāgena peṣayet | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.6]
anenābhyaktanayano naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.7]
rātrikaumudīṣu ca dīpikāsaṃbādhe suraṅgayā vā | [KāSū, 5, 6 10.8]
tatraitad bhavati | [KāSū, 5, 6 11.1]
dravyāṇām api nirhāre pānakānāṃ praveśane | [KāSū, 5, 6 11.2]
āpānakotsavārthe api ceṭikānāṃ ca saṃbhrame | [KāSū, 5, 6 11.3]
vyatyāse veśmanāṃ caiva rakṣiṇāṃ ca viparyaye | [KāSū, 5, 6 12.1]
udyānayātrāgamane yātrātaśca praveśane | [KāSū, 5, 6 12.2]
dīrghakālodayāṃ yātrāṃ proṣite cāpi rājani | [KāSū, 5, 6 13.1]
praveśanaṃ bhavet prāyo yūnāṃ niṣkramaṇaṃ tathā | [KāSū, 5, 6 13.2]
parasparasya kāryāṇi jñātvā cāntaḥpurālayāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 14.1]
ekakāryāstataḥ kuryuḥ śeṣāṇām api bhedanam | [KāSū, 5, 6 14.2]
dūṣayitvā tato 'nyonyam ekakāryārpaṇe sthiraḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 15.1]
abhedyatāṃ gataḥ sadyo yatheṣṭaṃ phalam aśnute | [KāSū, 5, 6 15.2]
tatra rājakulacāriṇya eva lakṣaṇyān puruṣān antaḥpuraṃ praveśayanti nātisurakṣatvād āparāntikānām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.1]
kṣatriyasaṃjñakair antaḥpurarakṣibhir evārthaṃ sādhayantyābhīrakāṇām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.2]
preṣyābhiḥ saha tadveṣān nāgarakaputrān praveśayanti vātsagulmakānām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.3]
svair eva putrair antaḥpurāṇi kāmacārair jananīvarjam upayujyante vaidarbhakāṇām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.4]
tathā praveśibhir eva jñātisaṃbandhibhir nānyair upayujyante strairājakānām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.5]
brāhmaṇair mitrair bhṛtyair dāsaceṭaiśca gauḍānām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.6]
parispandāḥ karmakarāścāntaḥpureṣvaniṣiddhā anye api tadrūpāśca saindhavānām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.7]
arthena rakṣiṇam upagṛhya sāhasikāḥ saṃhatāḥ praviśanti haimavatānām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.8]
puṣpadānaniyogān nagarabrāhmaṇā rājaviditam antaḥpurāṇi gacchanti | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.9]
paṭāntaritaiścaiṣām ālāpaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.10]
tena prasaṅgena vyatikaro bhavati vaṅgāṅgakaliṅgakānām | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.11]
saṃhatya navadaśetyekaikaṃ yuvānaṃ pracchādayanti prācyānām iti | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.12]
evaṃ parastriyaḥ prakurvīta | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.13]
ityantaḥpurikāvṛttam | [KāSū, 5, 6 16.14]
ebhya eva ca kāraṇebhyaḥ svadārān rakṣet | [KāSū, 5, 6 17.1]
kāmopadhāśuddhān rakṣiṇo 'ntaḥpure sthāpayed ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 18.1]
te hi bhayena cārthena cānyaṃ prayojayeyustasmāt kāmabhayārthopadhāśuddhān iti goṇikāputraḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 18.2]
adroho dharmastam api bhayājjahyād ato dharmabhayopadhāśuddhān iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 18.3]
paravākyābhidhāyinībhiśca gūḍhākārābhiḥ pramadābhir ātmadārān upadadhyācchaucāśaucaparijñānārtham iti bābhravīyāḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 19.1]
duṣṭānāṃ yuvatiṣu siddhatvān nākasmād aduṣṭadūṣaṇam ācared iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 19.2]
atigoṣṭhī niraṅkuśatvaṃ bhartuḥ svairatā puruṣaiḥ sahāniyantraṇatā | [KāSū, 5, 6 20.1]
pravāse avasthānaṃ videśe nivāsaḥ svavṛttyupaghātaḥ svairiṇīsaṃsargaḥ patyur īrṣyālutā ceti strīṇāṃ vināśakāraṇāni | [KāSū, 5, 6 20.2]
saṃdṛśya śāstrato yogān pāradārikalakṣitān | [KāSū, 5, 6 21.1]
na yāti chalanāṃ kaścit svadārān prati śāstravit | [KāSū, 5, 6 21.2]
pākṣikatvāt prayogāṇām apāyānāṃ ca darśanāt | [KāSū, 5, 6 22.1]
dharmārthayośca vailomyān nācaret pāradārikam | [KāSū, 5, 6 22.2]
tad etad dāraguptyartham ārabdhaṃ śreyase nṛṇām | [KāSū, 5, 6 22.3]
prajānāṃ dūṣaṇāyaiva na vijñeyo 'sya saṃvidhiḥ | [KāSū, 5, 6 22.4]
{KāSū, 6, 1}
veśyānāṃ puruṣādhigame ratir vṛttiśca sargāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.1]
ratitaḥ pravartanaṃ svābhāvikaṃ kṛtrimam arthārtham | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.2]
tad api svābhāvikavad rūpayet | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.3]
kāmaparāsu hi puṃsāṃ viśvāsayogāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.4]
alubdhatāṃ ca khyāpayet tasya nidarśanārtham | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.5]
na cānupāyenārthān sādhayed āyatisaṃrakṣaṇārtham | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.6]
nityam alaṃkārayoginī rājamārgāvalokinī dṛśyamānā na cātivivṛtā tiṣṭhet | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.7]
paṇyasadharmatvāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 1.8]
yair nāyakam āvarjayed anyābhyaś cāvacchindyād ātmanaścānarthaṃ pratikuryād arthaṃ ca sādhayen na ca gamyaiḥ paribhūyeta tān sahāyān kuryāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 2.1]
te tv ārakṣakapuruṣā dharmādhikaraṇasthā daivajñā vikrāntāḥ śūrāḥ samānavidyāḥ kalāgrāhiṇaḥ pīṭhamardaviṭavidūṣakamālākāragandhikaśauṇḍikarajakanāpitabhikṣukās te ca te ca kāryayogāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 2.2]
kevalārthāstvamī gamyāḥ svatantraḥ pūrve vayasi vartamāno vittavān aparokṣavṛttir adhikaraṇavān akṛcchrādhigatavittaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 3.1]
saṃgharṣavān saṃtatāyaḥ subhagamānī ślāghanakaḥ ṣaṇḍakaśca puṃśabdārthī | [KāSū, 6, 1 3.2]
samānaspardhī svabhāvatastyāgī | [KāSū, 6, 1 3.3]
rājani mahāmātre vā siddho daivapramāṇo vittāvamānī gurūṇāṃ śāsanātigaḥ sajātānāṃ lakṣyabhūtaḥ savitta ekaputro liṅgī pracchannakāmaḥ śūro vaidyaśceti | [KāSū, 6, 1 3.4]
prītiyaśo'rthāstu guṇato 'dhigamyāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 4.1]
mahākulīno viddhān sarvasamayajñaḥ kavir ākhyānakuśalo vāgmī pragalbho vividhaśilpajño vṛddhadarśī sthūlalakṣo mahotsāho dṛḍhabhaktir anasūyakastyāgī mitravatsalo ghaṭāgoṣṭhīprekṣaṇakasamājasamasyākrīḍanaśīlo nīrujo 'vyaṅgaśarīraḥ prāṇavānamadyapo vṛṣo maitraḥ strīṇāṃ praṇetā lālayitā ca | [KāSū, 6, 1 5.1]
na cāsāṃ vaśagaḥ svatantravṛttir aniṣṭhuro 'nīrṣyālur anavaśaṅkī ceti nāyakaguṇāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 5.2]
nāyikāyāḥ punā rūpayauvanalakṣaṇamādhuryayoginī guṇeṣvanuraktā na tathārtheṣu prītisaṃyogaśīlā sthiram atirekajātīyā viśeṣārthinī nityam akadaryavṛttir goṣṭhīkalāpriyā ceti | [KāSū, 6, 1 6.1]
nāyikā punarbuddhiśīlācāra ārjavaṃ kṛtajñatā dīrghadūradarśitvaṃ avisaṃvāditā deśakālajñatā nāgarakatā dainyātihāsapaiśunyaparivādakrodhalobhastambhacāpalavarjanaṃ pūrvābhibhāṣitā kāmasūtrakauśalaṃ tadaṅgavidyāsu ceti sādhāraṇaguṇāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 7.1]
guṇaviparyaye doṣāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 7.2]
kṣayī rogī kṛmiśakṛdvāyasāsyaḥ priyakalatraḥ paruṣavāk kadaryo nirghṛṇo gurujanaparityaktaḥ steno dambhaśīlo mūlakarmaṇi prasakto mānāpamānayor anapekṣī dveṣyair apyarthahāryo vilajja ityagamyāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 8.1]
rāgo bhayam arthaḥ saṃgharṣo vairaniryātanaṃ jijñāsā pakṣaḥ khedo gharmo yaśo 'nukampā suhṛdvākyaṃ hrīḥ priyasādṛśyaṃ dhanyatā rāgāpanayaḥ sājātyaṃ sāhaveśyaṃ sātatyam āyatiśca gamanakāraṇāni bhavantītyācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 9.1]
artho 'narthapratīghātaḥ prītiśceti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 9.2]
arthastu prītyā na bādhitaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 9.3]
asya prādhānyāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 9.4]
bhayādiṣu tu gurulāghavaṃ parīkṣyam iti sahāyagamyāgamyakāraṇacintā | [KāSū, 6, 1 9.5]
upamantritāpi gamyena sahasā na pratijānīyāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 10.1]
puruṣāṇāṃ sulabhāvamānitvāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 10.2]
bhāvajijñāsārthaṃ paricārakamukhān saṃvāhakagāyanavaihāsikān gamye tadbhaktān vā praṇidadhyāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 10.3]
tadabhāve pīṭhamardādīn | [KāSū, 6, 1 10.4]
tebhyo nāyakasya śaucāśaucaṃ rāgāparāgau saktāsaktāṃ dānādāne ca vidyāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 10.5]
saṃbhāvitena ca saha viṭapurogāṃ prītiṃ yojayet | [KāSū, 6, 1 10.6]
lāvakakukkuṭameṣayuddhaśukaśārikāpralāpanaprekṣaṇakakalāvyapadeśena pīṭhamardo nāyakaṃ tasyā udavasitam ānayet | [KāSū, 6, 1 11.1]
tāṃ vā tasya | [KāSū, 6, 1 11.2]
āgatasya prītikautukajananaṃ kiṃcid dravyajātaṃ svayam idam asādhāraṇopabhogyam iti prītidāyaṃ dadyāt | [KāSū, 6, 1 11.3]
yatra ca ramate tayā goṣṭhyainam upacāraiśca rañjayet | [KāSū, 6, 1 11.4]
gate ca saparihāsapralāpāṃ sopāyanāṃ paricārikām abhīkṣṇaṃ preṣayet | [KāSū, 6, 1 12.1]
sapīṭhamardāyāśca kāraṇāpadeśena svayaṃ gamanam iti gamyopāvartanam | [KāSū, 6, 1 12.2]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 13.1]
tāmbūlāni srajaścaiva saṃskṛtaṃ cānulepanam | [KāSū, 6, 1 13.2]
āgatasyāharet prītyā kalāgoṣṭhīśca yojayet | [KāSū, 6, 1 13.3]
dravyāṇi praṇaye dadyāt kuryācca parivartanam | [KāSū, 6, 1 14.1]
saṃprayogasya cākūtaṃ nijenaiva prayojayet | [KāSū, 6, 1 14.2]
prītidāyair upanyāsair upacāraiśca kevalaiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 1 15.1]
gamyena saha saṃsṛṣṭā rañjayet taṃ tataḥ param | [KāSū, 6, 1 15.2]
{KāSū, 6, 2}
saṃyuktā nāyakena tadrañjanārtham ekacāriṇīvṛttam anutiṣṭhet | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.1]
rañjayenna tu sajjeta saktavacca viceṣṭeteti saṃkṣepoktiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.2]
mātari ca krūraśīlāyām arthaparāyāṃ cāyattā syāt | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.3]
tadabhāve mātṛkāyām | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.4]
sā tu gamyena nātiprīyeta | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.5]
prasahya ca duhitaram ānayet | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.6]
tatra tu nāyikāyāḥ saṃtatam aratir nirvedo vrīḍābhayaṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.7]
na tv eva śāsanātivṛttiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.8]
vyādhiṃ caikam animittam ajugupsitam acakṣurgrāhyam anityaṃ ca khyāpayet | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.9]
sati kāraṇe tadapadeśaṃ ca nāyakān abhigamanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.10]
nirmālyasya tu nāyikā ceṭikāṃ preṣayet tāmbūlasya ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 1.11]
vyavāye tadupacāreṣu vismayaś catuḥṣaṣṭyāṃ śiṣyatvaṃ tadupadiṣṭānāṃ ca yogānām ābhīkṣṇyenānuyogas tatsātmyād rahasi vṛttir manorathānām ākhyānaṃ guhyānāṃ vaikṛtapracchādanaṃ śayane parāvṛttasyānupekṣaṇam ānulomyaṃ guhyasparśane suptasya cumbanam āliṅganaṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 2.1]
prekṣaṇam anyamanaskasya | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.1]
rājamārge ca prāsādasthāyāstatra viditāyā vrīḍāśāṭhyanāśaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.2]
taddveṣye dveṣyatā | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.3]
tatpriye priyatā | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.4]
tam anu harṣaśokau | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.5]
strīṣu jijñāsā | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.6]
kopaścādīrghaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.7]
svakṛteṣvapi nakhadaśanacihneṣvanyāśaṅkā | [KāSū, 6, 2 3.8]
anurāgasyāvacanam ākāratastu darśayet | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.1]
madasvapnavyādhiṣu tu nirvacanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.2]
ślāghyānāṃ nāyakakarmaṇāṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.3]
tasmin bruvāṇe vākyārthagrahaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.4]
tadavadhārya praśaṃsāviṣaye bhāṣaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.5]
tadvākyasya cottareṇa yojanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.6]
bhaktimāṃścet | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.7]
kathāsvanuvṛttir anyatra sapatnyāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.8]
niḥśvāse jṛmbhite skhalite patite vā tasya cārtim āśaṃsīta | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.9]
kṣutavyāhṛtavismiteṣu jīvetyudāharaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.10]
daurmanasye vyādhidaurhṛdāpadeśaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.11]
guṇataḥ parasyākīrtanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.12]
na nindā samānadoṣasya | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.13]
dattasya dhāraṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.14]
vṛthāparādhe tadvyasane vālaṃkārasyāgrahaṇam abhojanaṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.15]
tadyuktāśca vilāpāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.16]
tena saha deśamokṣaṃ rocayed rājani niṣkrayaṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.17]
sāmarthyam āyuṣastadavāptau | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.18]
tasyārthādhigame abhipretasiddhau śarīropacaye vā pūrvasaṃbhāṣita iṣṭadevatopahāraḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.19]
nityam alaṃkārayogaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.20]
parimito 'bhyavahāraḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.21]
gīte ca nāmagotrayor grahaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.22]
glānyām urasi lalāṭe ca karaṃ kurvīta | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.23]
tatsukham upalabhya nidrālābhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.24]
utsaṅge cāsyopaveśanaṃ svapanaṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.25]
gamanaṃ viyoge | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.26]
tasmāt putrārthinī syāt | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.27]
āyuṣo nādhikyam icchet | [KāSū, 6, 2 4.28]
etasyāvijñātam arthaṃ rahasi na brūyāt | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.1]
vratam upavāsaṃ cāsya nirvartayet mayi doṣa iti | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.2]
aśakye svayam api tadrūpā syāt | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.3]
vivāde tenāpyaśakyam ityarthanirdeśaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.4]
tadīyam ātmīyaṃ vā svayam aviśeṣeṇa paśyet | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.5]
tena vinā goṣṭhyādīnām agamanam iti | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.6]
nirmālyadhāraṇe ślāghā ucchiṣṭabhojane ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.7]
kulaśīlaśilpajātividyāvarṇavittadeśamitraguṇavayomādhuryapūjā | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.8]
gītādiṣu codanam abhijñasya | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.9]
bhayaśītoṣṇavarṣāṇy anapekṣya tadabhigamanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.10]
sa eva ca me syād ityaurdhvadehikeṣu vacanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.11]
tadiṣṭarasabhāvaśīlānuvartanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.12]
mūlakarmābhiśaṅkā | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.13]
tadabhigamane ca jananyā saha nityo vivādaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.14]
balāt kāreṇa ca yadyanyatra tayā nīyeta tadā viṣamanaśanaṃ śastraṃ rajjum iti kāmayeta | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.15]
pratyāyanaṃ ca praṇidhibhir nāyakasya | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.16]
svayaṃ vātmano vṛttigrahaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.17]
na tv evārtheṣu vivādaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.18]
mātrā vinā kiṃcin na ceṣṭeta | [KāSū, 6, 2 5.19]
pravāse śīghrāgamanāya śāpadānam | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.1]
proṣite mṛjāniyamaścālaṃkārasya pratiṣedhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.2]
maṅgalaṃ tvapekṣyam | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.3]
ekaṃ śaṅkhavalayaṃ vā dhārayet | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.4]
smaraṇam atītānām | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.5]
nakṣatracandrasūryatārābhyaḥ spṛhaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.6]
iṣṭasvapnadarśane tatsaṃgamo mamāstv iti vacanam | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.7]
udvego 'niṣṭe śāntikarma ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.8]
pratyāgate kāmapūjā | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.9]
devatopahārāṇāṃ karaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.10]
sakhībhiḥ pūrṇapātrasyāharaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.11]
vāyasapūjā ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.12]
prathamasamāgamānantaraṃ caitad eva vāyasapūjāvarjam | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.13]
saktasya cānumaraṇaṃ brūyāt | [KāSū, 6, 2 6.14]
nisṛṣṭabhāvaḥ samānavṛttiḥ prayojanakārī nirāśaṅko nirapekṣo 'rtheṣv iti saktalakṣaṇāni | [KāSū, 6, 2 7.1]
tad etan nirdarśanārthaṃ dattakaśāsanād uktam | [KāSū, 6, 2 8.1]
anuktaṃ ca lokataḥ śīlayet puruṣaprakṛtitaśca | [KāSū, 6, 2 8.2]
bhavataścātra ślokau | [KāSū, 6, 2 9.1]
sūkṣmatvād atilobhācca prakṛtyājñānatastathā | [KāSū, 6, 2 9.2]
kāmalakṣma tu durjñānaṃ strīṇāṃ tadbhāvitair api | [KāSū, 6, 2 9.3]
kāmayante virajyante rañjayanti tyajanti ca | [KāSū, 6, 2 10.1]
karṣayantyo 'pi sarvārthāñ jñāyante naiva yoṣitaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 2 10.2]
{KāSū, 6, 3}
saktādivittādānaṃ svābhāvikam upāyataśca | [KāSū, 6, 3 1.1]
tatra svābhāvikaṃ saṃkalpāt samadhikaṃ vā labhamānā nopāyān prayuñjītetyācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 1.2]
viditam apyupāyaiḥ pariṣkṛtaṃ dviguṇaṃ dāsyatīti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 1.3]
alaṃkārabhakṣyabhojyapeyamālyavastragandhadravyādīnāṃ vyavahāriṣu kālikam uddhārārtham arthapratinayanena | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.1]
tatsamakṣaṃ tadvittapraśaṃsā | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.2]
vratavṛkṣārāmadevakulataḍāgodyānotsavaprītidāyavyapadeśaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.3]
tadabhigamananimitto rakṣibhiścaurair vālaṃkāraparimoṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.4]
dāhāt kuḍyacchedāt pramādād bhavane cārthanāśaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.5]
tathā yācitālaṃkārāṇāṃ nāyakālaṃkārāṇāṃ ca tadabhigamanārthasya vyayasya praṇidhibhir nivedanam | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.6]
tadartham ṛṇagrahaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.7]
suhṛtkāryeṣvanabhigamanam anabhihārahetoḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.8]
taiśca pūrvam āhṛtā guravo 'bhihārāḥ pūrvam upanītāḥ pūrvaṃ śrāvitāḥ syuḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.9]
ucitānāṃ kriyāṇāṃ vicchittiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.10]
nāyakārthaṃ ca śilpiṣu kāryam | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.11]
vaidyamahāmātrayor upakārikriyā kāryahetoḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.12]
mitrāṇāṃ copakāriṇāṃ vyasaneṣvabhyupapattiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.13]
gṛhakarma | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.14]
sakhyāḥ putrasyotsañjanam dohado vyādhir mitrasya duḥkhāpanayanam iti | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.15]
alaṃkāraikadeśavikrayo nāyakasyārthe | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.16]
tayā śīlitasya cālaṃkārasya bhāṇḍopaskarasya vā vaṇijo vikrayārthaṃ darśanam | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.17]
pratigaṇikānāṃ ca sadṛśasya bhāṇḍasya vyatikare prativiśiṣṭasya grahaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.18]
pūrvopakārāṇām avismaraṇam anukīrtanaṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.19]
praṇidhibhiḥ pratigaṇikānāṃ lābhātiśayaṃ śrāvayet | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.20]
tāsu nāyakasamakṣam ātmano 'bhyadhikaṃ lābhaṃ bhūtam abhūtaṃ vā vrīḍitā nāma varṇayet | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.21]
pūrvayogināṃ ca lābhātiśayena punaḥ saṃdhāne yatamānānām āviṣkṛtaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.22]
tatspardhināṃ tyāgayogināṃ nidarśanam | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.23]
na punar eṣyatīti bālayācitakam ityarthāgamopāyāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 2.24]
viraktaṃ ca nityam eva prakṛtivikriyāto vidyāt mukhavarṇācca | [KāSū, 6, 3 3.1]
ūnam atiriktaṃ vā dadāti | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.1]
pratilomaiḥ sambadhyate | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.2]
vyapadiśyānyat karoti | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.3]
ucitam ācchinatti | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.4]
pratijñātam vismarati | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.5]
svapakṣaiḥ saṃjñayā bhāṣate | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.6]
mitrakāryam apadiśyānyatra śete | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.7]
pūrvasaṃsṛṣṭāyāśca parijanena mithaḥ kathayati | [KāSū, 6, 3 4.8]
tasya sāradravyāṇi prāg avabodhād anyāpadeśena haste kurvīta | [KāSū, 6, 3 5.1]
tāni cāsyā hastād uttamarṇaḥ prasahya gṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 6, 3 5.2]
vivadamānena saha dharmastheṣu vyavahared iti viraktapratipattiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 5.3]
saktaṃ tu pūrvopakāriṇam apyalpaphalaṃ vyalīkenānupālayet | [KāSū, 6, 3 6.1]
asāraṃ tu niṣpratipattikam upāyayo 'pavāhayet | [KāSū, 6, 3 6.2]
anyam avaṣṭabhya | [KāSū, 6, 3 6.3]
ninditābhyāsaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 7.2]
oṣṭhanirbhogaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 7.3]

āhatya cāsya kathām anyāḥ kathāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 3 9.4]

{KāSū, 6, 4}
vartamānaṃ niṣpīḍitārtham utsṛjantī pūrvasaṃsṛṣṭena saha saṃdadhyāt | [KāSū, 6, 4 1.1]
sa ced avasitārtho vittavān sānurāgaśca tataḥ saṃdheyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 2.1]
anyatra gatastarkayitavyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 3.1]
sa kāryayuktyā ṣaḍvidhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 3.2]
itaḥ svayam apasṛtas tato 'pi svayam evāpasṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 4.1]
itastataśca niṣkāsitāpasṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 4.2]
itaḥ svayam apasṛtastato niṣkāsitāpasṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 4.3]
itaḥ svayam apasṛtastatra sthitaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 4.4]
ito niṣkāsitāpasṛtastataḥ svayam apasṛtaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 4.5]
ito niṣkāsitāpasṛtastatra sthitaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 4.6]
itastataśca svayam evāpasṛtyopajapati ced ubhayor guṇān apekṣī calabuddhir asaṃdheyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 5.1]
itastataśca niṣkāsitāpasṛtaḥ sthirabuddhiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 6.1]
sa ced anyato bahulabhamānayā niṣkāsitaḥ syāt sasāro 'pi tayā roṣito mamāmarṣād bahu dāsyatīti saṃdheyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 6.2]
niḥsāratayā kadaryatayā vā tyakto na śreyān | [KāSū, 6, 4 7.1]
itaḥ svayam apasṛtastato niṣkāsitāpasṛto yadyatiriktam ādau ca dadyāt tataḥ pratigrāhyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 8.1]
itaḥ svayam apasṛtya tatra sthita upajapaṃstarkayitavyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 9.1]
viśeṣārthī cāgatastato viśeṣam apaśyann āgantukāmo māṃ jijñāsitukāmaḥ sa āgatya sānurāgatvād dāsyati | [KāSū, 6, 4 10.1]
tasyāṃ vā doṣān dṛṣṭvā mayi bhūyiṣṭhān guṇān adhunā paśyati sa guṇadarśī bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dāsyati | [KāSū, 6, 4 10.2]
bālo vā naikatradṛṣṭir atisaṃdhānapradhāno vā haridrārāgo vā yat kiṃcanakārī vā ityavetya saṃdadhyān na vā | [KāSū, 6, 4 11.1]
ito niṣkāsitāpasṛtastataḥ svayam apasṛta upajapaṃstarkayitavyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 12.1]
anurāgād āgantukāmaḥ sa bahu dāsyati | [KāSū, 6, 4 12.2]
mama guṇair bhāvito yo 'nyasyāṃ na ramate | [KāSū, 6, 4 12.3]
pūrvam ayogena vā mayā niṣkāsitaḥ sa māṃ śīlayitvā vairaṃ niryātayitukāmo dhanam abhiyogād vā mayāsyāpahṛtaṃ tadviśvāsya pratīpam ādātukāmo nirveṣṭukāmo vā māṃ vartamānodbhedayitvā tyaktukāma ityakalyāṇabuddhir asaṃdheyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 13.1]
anyathābuddhiḥ kālena lambhayitavyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 14.1]
ito niṣkāsitastatra sthita upajapann etena vyākhyātaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 15.1]
teṣu upajapatsvanyatra sthitaḥ svayam upajapet | [KāSū, 6, 4 16.1]
vyalīkārthaṃ niṣkāsito mayāsāvanyatra gato yatnād ānetavyaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.1]
itaḥ pravṛttasaṃbhāṣo vā tato bhedam avāpsyati | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.2]
vartamānasya ced arthavighātaṃ kariṣyati | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.3]
arthāgamakālo vāsya | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.4]
sthānavṛddhir asya jātā | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.5]
labdham anenādhikaraṇam | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.6]
dārair viyuktaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.7]
pāratantryād vyāvṛttaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.8]
pitrā bhrātrā vā vibhaktaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.9]
anena vā pratibaddham anena saṃdhiṃ kṛtvā nāyakaṃ dhaninam avāpsyāmi | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.10]
vimānito vā bhāryayā tam eva tasyāṃ vikramayiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.11]
asya vā mitraṃ maddveṣiṇīṃ sapatnīṃ kāmayate tad amunā bhedayiṣyāmi | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.12]
calacittatayā vā lāghavam enam āpādayiṣyāmīti | [KāSū, 6, 4 17.13]
tasya pīṭhamardādayo mātur dauḥśīlyena nāyikāyāḥ satyapyanurāge vivaśāyāḥ pūrvaṃ niṣkāsanaṃ varṇayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 18.1]
vartamānena cākāmāyāḥ saṃsargaṃ vidveṣaṃ ca | [KāSū, 6, 4 18.2]
tasyāśca sābhijñānaiḥ pūrvānurāgair enaṃ pratyāpayeyuḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 18.3]
abhijñānaṃ ca tatkṛtopakārasambaddhaṃ syād iti viśīrṇapratisaṃdhānam | [KāSū, 6, 4 18.4]
apūrvapūrvasaṃsṛṣṭayoḥ pūrvasaṃsṛṣṭaḥ śreyān | [KāSū, 6, 4 19.1]
sa hi viditaśīlo dṛṣṭarāgaśca sūpacāro bhavatītyācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 19.2]
pūrvasaṃsṛṣṭaḥ sarvato niṣpīḍitārthatvān nātyartham arthado duḥkhaṃ ca punarviśvāsayitum | [KāSū, 6, 4 19.3]
apūrvastu sukhenānurajyata iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 19.4]
tathāpi puruṣaprakṛtito viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 19.5]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 20.1]
anyāṃ bhedayituṃ gamyād anyato gamyam eva vā | [KāSū, 6, 4 20.2]
sthitasya copaghātārthaṃ punaḥ saṃdhānam iṣyate | [KāSū, 6, 4 20.3]
bibhetyanyasya saṃyogād vyalīkāni ca nekṣate | [KāSū, 6, 4 21.1]
atisaktaḥ pumān yatra bhayād bahu dadāti ca | [KāSū, 6, 4 21.2]
asaktam abhinandeta saktaṃ paribhavet tathā | [KāSū, 6, 4 22.1]
anyadūtānupāte ca yaḥ syād ativiśāradaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 4 22.2]
tatropayāyinaṃ pūrvaṃ nārī kālena yojayet | [KāSū, 6, 4 23.1]
bhaveccācchinnasaṃdhānā na ca saktaṃ parityajet | [KāSū, 6, 4 23.2]
saktaṃ tu vaśinaṃ nārī sambhāṣyāpyanyato vrajet | [KāSū, 6, 4 24.1]
tataścārtham upādāya saktam evānurañjayet | [KāSū, 6, 4 24.2]
āyatiṃ prasamīkṣyādau lābhaṃ prītiṃ ca puṣkalām | [KāSū, 6, 4 25.1]
sauhṛdaṃ pratisaṃdadhyād viśīrṇaṃ strī vicakṣaṇā | [KāSū, 6, 4 25.2]
{KāSū, 6, 5}
gamyabāhulye bahu pratidinaṃ ca labhamānā naikaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 6, 5 1.1]
deśaṃ kālaṃ sthitim ātmano guṇān saubhāgyaṃ cānyābhyo nyūnātiriktatāṃ cāvekṣya rajanyām arthaṃ sthāpayet | [KāSū, 6, 5 2.1]
gamye dūtāṃśca prayojayet | [KāSū, 6, 5 3.1]
tatpratibaddhāṃśca svayaṃ prahiṇuyāt | [KāSū, 6, 5 3.2]
dvistriścatur iti lābhātiśayagrahārtham ekasyāpi gacchet | [KāSū, 6, 5 4.1]
parigrahaṃ ca caret | [KāSū, 6, 5 4.2]
gamyayaugapadye tu lābhasāmye yad dravyārthinī syāt taddāyini viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣa ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 5.1]
apratyādeyatvāt sarvakāryāṇāṃ tanmūlatvāddhiraṇyada iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 6.1]
suvarṇarajatatāmrakāṃsyalohabhāṇḍopaskarāstaraṇaprāvaraṇavāsoviśeṣagandhadravyakaṭukabhāṇḍaghṛtatailadhānyapaśujātīnāṃ pūrvapūrvato viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 7.1]
yat tatra sāmyād vā dravyasāmye mitravākyād atipātitvād āyatito gamyaguṇataḥ prītitaśca viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 7.2]
rāgityāginostyāgini viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣa ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 8.1]
śakyo hi rāgiṇi tyāga ādhātum | [KāSū, 6, 5 9.1]
lubdho 'pi hi raktastyajati na tu tyāgī nirbandhād rajyata iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 10.1]
tatrāpi dhanavadadhanavator dhanavati viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 11.1]
tyāgiprayojanakartroḥ prayojanakartari viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣa ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 11.2]
prayojanakartā sakṛt kṛtvā kṛtinam ātmānaṃ manyate tyāgī punar atītaṃ nāpekṣata iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 12.1]
tatrāpyātyayikato viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 13.1]
kṛtajñatyāginostyāgini viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣa ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 13.2]
ciram ārādhito 'pi tyāgī vyalīkam ekam upalabhya pratigaṇikayā vā mithyādūṣitaḥ śramam atītaṃ nāpekṣate | [KāSū, 6, 5 14.1]
prāyeṇa hi tejasvina ṛjavo 'nādṛtāśca tyāgino bhavanti | [KāSū, 6, 5 14.2]
kṛtajñastu pūrvaśramāpekṣī na sahasā virajyate | [KāSū, 6, 5 14.3]
parīkṣitaśīlatvācca na mithyā dūṣyata iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 14.4]
tatrāpyāyatito viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 15.1]
mitravacanārthāgamayor arthāgame viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣa ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 16.1]
so 'pi hyarthāgamo bhavitā | [KāSū, 6, 5 17.1]
mitraṃ tu sakṛd vākye pratihate kaluṣitaṃ syād iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 17.2]
tatrāpyatipātato viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 18.1]
tatra kāryasaṃdarśanena mitram anunīya śvobhūte vacanam astv iti tato 'tipātinam arthaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 6, 5 19.1]
arthāgamānarthapratīghātayor arthāgame viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣa ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 20.1]
arthaḥ parimitāvacchedaḥ anarthaḥ punaḥ sakṛtprasṛto na jñāyate kvāvatiṣṭhata iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 21.1]
tatrāpi gurulāghavakṛto viśeṣaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 22.1]
etenārthasaṃśayād anarthapratīkāre viśeṣo vyākhyātaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 23.1]
devakulataḍāgārāmāṇām karaṇam sthalīnām agnicaityānāṃ nibandhanam gosahasrāṇāṃ pātrāntaritaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo dānam devatānāṃ pūjopahārapravartanam tadvyayasahiṣṇor vā dhanasya parigrahaṇam ityuttamagaṇikānāṃ lābhātiśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 24.1]
sārvāṅgiko 'laṃkārayogo gṛhasyodārasya karaṇam | [KāSū, 6, 5 25.1]
mahārhair bhāṇḍaiḥ paricārakaiśca gṛhaparicchadasyojjvalateti rūpājīvānāṃ lābhātiśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 25.2]
nityaṃ śuklam ācchādanam apakṣudham annapānaṃ nityaṃ saugandhikena tāmbūlena ca yogaḥ sahiraṇyabhāgam alaṃkaraṇam iti kumbhadāsīnāṃ lābhātiśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 26.1]
etena pradeśena madhyamādhamānām api lābhātiśayān sarvāsām eva yojayed ityācāryāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 27.1]
deśakālavibhavasāmarthyānurāgalokapravṛttivaśād aniyatalābhādiyamavṛttir iti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 28.1]
gamyam anyato nivārayitukāmā saktam anyasyām apahartukāmā vā anyāṃ vā lābhato viyuyukṣamāṇāgamyasaṃsargād ātmanaḥ sthānaṃ vṛddhim āyatim abhigamyatāṃ ca manyamānā anarthapratīkāre vā sāhāyam enaṃ kārayitukāmā saktasya vā anyasya vyalīkārthinī pūrvopakāram akṛtam iva paśyantī kevala prītyarthinī vā kalyāṇabuddher alpam api lābhaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 6, 5 29.1]
āyatyarthinī tu tam āśritya cānarthaṃ praticikīrṣantī naiva pratigṛhṇīyāt | [KāSū, 6, 5 30.1]
tyakṣyāmyenam anyataḥ pratisaṃdhāsyāmi gamiṣyati dārair yokṣyate nāśayiṣyatyanarthān aṅkuśabhūta uttarādhyakṣo 'syāgamiṣyati svāmī pitā vā sthānabhraṃśo vāsya bhaviṣyati calacittaśceti manyamānā tadātve tasmāl lābham icchet | [KāSū, 6, 5 31.1]
pratijñātam īśvareṇa pratigrahaṃ lapsyate adhikaraṇaṃ sthānaṃ vā prāpsyati vṛttikālo 'sya vā āsannaḥ vāhanam asyā gamiṣyati sthalapattraṃ vā sasyam asya pakṣyate kṛtam asmin na naśyati nityam avisaṃvādako vetyāyatyām icchet | [KāSū, 6, 5 32.1]
parigrahakalpaṃ vācaret | [KāSū, 6, 5 32.2]
bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 33.1]
kṛcchrādhigatavittāṃśca rājavallabhaniṣṭhurān | [KāSū, 6, 5 33.2]
āyātyāṃ ca tadātve ca dūrād eva vivarjayet | [KāSū, 6, 5 33.3]
anartho varjane yeṣāṃ gamane abhyudayastathā | [KāSū, 6, 5 34.1]
prayatnenāpi tān gṛhya sāpadeśam upakramet | [KāSū, 6, 5 34.2]
prasannā ye prayacchanti svalpe apyagaṇitaṃ vasu | [KāSū, 6, 5 35.1]
sthūlalakṣān mahotsāhāṃstān gacchet svair api vyayaiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 5 35.2]
{KāSū, 6, 6}
arthān ācaryamāṇān anarthā apyanūdbhavantyanubandhāḥ saṃśayāśca | [KāSū, 6, 6 1.1]
te buddhidaurbalyād atirāgād atyabhimānād atidambhād atyārjavād ativiśvāsād atikrodhāt pramādāt sāhasād daivayogācca syuḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 2.1]
teṣāṃ phalaṃ kṛtasya vyayasya niṣphalatvam anāyatirāgam iṣyato 'rthasya nivartanam āptasya niṣkramaṇaṃ pāruṣyasya prāptir gamyatā śarīrasya praghātaḥ keśānāṃ chedanaṃ pātanam aṅgavaikalyāpattiḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 3.1]
tasmāt tān ādita eva parijihīrṣed arthabhūyiṣṭhāṃścopekṣeta | [KāSū, 6, 6 3.2]
artho dharmaḥ kāma ityarthatrivargaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 4.1]
anartho 'dharmo dveṣa ityanarthatrivargaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 4.2]
teṣv ācaryamāṇeṣvanyasyāpi niṣpattir anubandhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 4.3]
saṃdigdhāyāṃ tu phalaprāptau syād vā na veti śuddhasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 4.4]
idaṃ vā syād idaṃ veti saṃkīrṇaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 4.5]
ekasmin kriyamāṇe kārye kāryadvayasyotpattir ubhayato yogaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 4.6]
samantād utpattiḥ samantatoyoga iti tān udāhariṣyāmaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 4.7]
vicāritarūpo 'rthatrivargaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 5.1]
tadviparīta evānarthatrivargaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 5.2]
yasyottamasyābhigamane pratyakṣato 'rthalābho grahaṇīyatvam āyatir āgamaḥ prārthanīyatvaṃ cānyeṣāṃ syāt so 'rtho 'rthānubandhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 6.1]
lābhamātre kasyacid anyasya gamanaṃ so 'rtho niranubandhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 7.1]
anyārthaparigrahe saktād āyaticchedanam arthasya niṣkramaṇaṃ lokavidviṣṭasya vā nīcasya gamanam āyatighnam artho 'narthānubandhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 8.1]
svena vyayena śūrasya mahāmātrasya prabhavato vā lubdhasya gamanaṃ niṣphalam api vyasanapratīkārārthaṃ mahataścārthaghnasya nimittasya praśamanam āyatijananaṃ vā so 'nartho 'rthānubandhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 9.1]
kadaryasya subhagamāninaḥ kṛtaghnasya vātisaṃdhānaśīlasya svair api vyayaistathārādhanam ante niṣphalaṃ so 'nartho niranubandhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 10.1]
tasyaiva rājavallabhasya krauryaprabhāvādhikasya tathaivārādhanam ante niṣphalaṃ niṣkāsanaṃ ca doṣakaraṃ so 'nartho 'narthānubandhaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 11.1]
evaṃ dharmakāmayor apyanubandhān yojayet | [KāSū, 6, 6 12.1]
paraspareṇa ca yuktyā saṃkired ityanubandhāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 13.1]
paritoṣito 'pi dāsyati na vetyarthasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 14.1]
niṣpīḍitārtham aphalam utsṛjantyā artham alabhamānāyā dharmaḥ syān na veti dharmasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 14.2]
abhipretam upalabhya paricārakam anyaṃ vā kṣudraṃ gatvā kāmaḥ syān na veti kāmasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 14.3]
prabhāvavān kṣudro 'nabhimato 'narthaṃ kariṣyati na vetyanarthasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 14.4]
atyantaniṣphalaḥ saktaḥ parityaktaḥ pitṛlokaṃ yāyāt tatrādharmaḥ syān na vetyadharmasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 14.5]
rāgasyāpi vivakṣāyām abhipretam anupalabhya virāgaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 14.6]
iti śuddhasaṃśayāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 14.7]
atha saṃkīrṇāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 15.1]
āgantor aviditaśīlasya vallabhasaṃśrayasya prabhaviṣṇor vā samupasthitasyārādhanam artho 'nartha iti saṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 16.1]
śrotriyasya brahmacāriṇo dīkṣitasya vratino liṅgino vā māṃ dṛṣṭvā jātarāgasya mumūrṣor mitravākyād ānṛśaṃsyācca gamanaṃ dharmo 'dharma iti saṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 16.2]
lokād evākṛtapratyayād aguṇo guṇavān vety anavekṣya gamanaṃ kāmo dveṣa iti saṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 16.3]
saṃkirecca paraspareṇeti saṃkīrṇasaṃśayāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 16.4]
yatra parasyābhigamane arthaḥ saktācca saṃgharṣataḥ sa ubhayayo 'rthaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 17.1]
yatra svena vyayena niṣphalam abhigamanaṃ saktāccāmarṣitād vittapratyādānaṃ sa ubhayato 'narthaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 17.2]
yatrābhigamane artho bhaviṣyati na vetyāśaṅkā sakto 'pi saṃgharṣād dāsyati na veti sa ubhayato 'rthasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 17.3]
yatrābhigamane vyayavati pūrvo viruddhaḥ krodhād apakāraṃ kariṣyati na veti sakto vāmarṣito dattaṃ pratyādāsyati na veti sa ubhayato 'narthasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 17.4]
ityauddālaker ubhayatoyogāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 17.5]
bābhravīyāstu | [KāSū, 6, 6 18.1]
yatrābhigamane artho 'nabhigamane ca saktād arthaḥ sa ubhayato 'rthaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 18.2]
yatrābhigamane niṣphalo vyayo 'nabhigamane ca niṣpratīkāro 'narthaḥ sa ubhayato 'narthaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 18.3]
yatrābhigamane nirvyayo dāsyati na veti saṃśayo 'nabhigamane sakto dāsyati na veti sa ubhayato 'rthasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 18.4]
yatrābhigamane vyayavati pūrvo viruddhaḥ prabhāvavān prāpsyate na veti saṃśayo 'nabhigamane ca krodhād anarthaṃ kariṣyati na veti sa ubhayato 'narthasaṃśayaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 18.5]
eteṣām eva vyatikare anyato 'rtho 'nyato 'nartho 'nyato 'rtho 'nyato 'rthasaṃśayo 'nyato 'rtho 'nyato 'narthasaṃśaya iti ṣaṭsaṃkīrṇayogāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 19.1]
teṣu sahāyaiḥ saha vimṛśya yato 'rthabhūyiṣṭho 'rthasaṃśayo gurur anarthapraśamo vā tataḥ pravarteta | [KāSū, 6, 6 20.1]
evaṃ dharmakāmavapyanayaiva yuktyodāharet | [KāSū, 6, 6 21.1]
saṃkirecca paraspareṇa vyatiṣañjayec cetyubhayatoyogāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 21.2]
sambhūya ca viṭāḥ parigṛhṇantyekām asau goṣṭhīparigrahaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 22.1]
sā teṣām itastataḥ saṃsṛjyamānā pratyekaṃ saṃgharṣād arthaṃ nirvartayet | [KāSū, 6, 6 22.2]
suvasantakādiṣu ca yoge yo me imam amuṃ ca saṃpādayiṣyati tasyādya gamiṣyati me duhiteti mātrā vācayet | [KāSū, 6, 6 22.3]
teṣāṃ ca saṃgharṣaje abhigamane kāryāṇi lakṣayet | [KāSū, 6, 6 22.4]
ekato 'rthaḥ sarvato 'rthaḥ ekato 'narthaḥ sarvato 'nartho 'rdhato 'rthaḥ sarvato 'rthaḥ ardhato 'narthaḥ sarvato 'narthaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 22.5]
iti samantato yogāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 22.6]
arthasaṃśayam anarthasaṃśayaṃ ca pūrvavad yojayet | [KāSū, 6, 6 23.1]
saṃkirecca tathā dharmakāmāvapi | [KāSū, 6, 6 23.2]
ity anubandhārthānarthasaṃśayavicārāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 23.3]
kumbhadāsī paricārikā kulaṭā svairiṇī naṭī śilpakārikā prakāśavinaṣṭā rūpājīvā gaṇikā ceti veśyāviśeṣāḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 24.1]
sarvāsāṃ cānurūpeṇa gamyāḥ sahāyāstad uparañjanam arthāgamopāyā niṣkāsanaṃ punaḥ sadhānaṃ lābhaviśeṣānubandhā arthānarthānubandhasaṃśayavicārāśceti vaiśikam | [KāSū, 6, 6 25.1]
bhavataścātra ślokau | [KāSū, 6, 6 26.1]
ratyarthāḥ puruṣā yena ratyarthāścaiva yoṣitaḥ | [KāSū, 6, 6 26.2]
śāstrasyārthapradhānatvāt tena yogo 'tra yoṣitām | [KāSū, 6, 6 27.1]
santi rāgaparā nāryaḥ santi cārthaparā api | [KāSū, 6, 6 28.1]
prāk tatra varṇito rāgo veśyāyogāśca vaiśike | [KāSū, 6, 6 28.2]
{KāSū, 7, 1}
vyākhyātaṃ ca kāmasūtraṃ | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.1]
tatroktaistu vidhibhir abhipretam artham anadhigacchan aupaniṣadikam ācaret | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.2]
rūpaṃ guṇo vayastyāga iti subhagaṃkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.3]
tagarakuṣṭhatālīsapatrakānulepanaṃ subhagaṃkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.4]
etair eva supiṣṭair vartim ālipyākṣatailena narakapāle sādhitam añjanaṃ ca | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.5]
punarnavāsahadevīsārivākuraṇṭotpalapatraiśca siddhaṃ tailam abhyañjanam | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.6]
tadyuktā eva srajaśca | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.7]
padmotpalanāgakesarāṇāṃ śoṣitānāṃ cūrṇaṃ madhughṛtābhyām avalihya subhago bhavati | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.8]
tānyeva tagaratālīsatamālapatrayuktāny anulepanam | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.9]
mayūrasyākṣitarakṣor vā suvarṇenālipya dakṣiṇahastena dhārayed iti subhagaṃkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.10]
tathā bādaraṃ maṇiṃ śaṅkhamaṇiṃ ca teṣāṃ cātharvaṇān yogān gamayet | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.11]
vidyātantrācca vidyāyogāt prāptayauvanāṃ paricārikāṃ svāmī saṃvatsaramātram anyato dhārayet | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.12]
tato dhāritāṃ bālāṃ matvā lālasībhūteṣu gamyeṣu yo 'syāḥ saṃharṣeṇa bahu dadyāt tasmai visṛjed iti saubhāgyavardhanam | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.13]
gaṇikā prāptayauvanāṃ svāṃ duhitaraṃ tasyā vijñānaśīlarūpānurūpyeṇa tān abhinimantrya sāreṇa yo 'syai idam idaṃ ca dadyāt sa pāṇiṃ gṛhṇīyād iti saṃsādhya rakṣayed iti | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.14]
sā ca māturaviditā nāma nāgarikaputrair dhanibhir atyarthaṃ prīyeta | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.15]
teṣāṃ kalāgrahaṇe gandharvaśālāyāṃ bhikṣukībhavane tatra tatra ca saṃdarśanayogāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.16]
teṣāṃ yathoktadāyināṃ mātā pāṇiṃ grāhayet | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.17]
tat tāvad artham alabhamānā tu svenāpyekadeśena duhitre etad dattam aneneti khyāpayet | [KāSū, 7, 1 1.18]
pracchannaṃ vā taiḥ saṃyojya svayam ajānatī bhūtvā tato viditeṣv evaṃ dharmastheṣu nivedayet | [KāSū, 7, 1 2.1]
sakhyaiva tu dāsyā vā mocitakanyābhāvām upagṛhītakāmasūtrām ābhyāsikeṣu yogeṣu pratiṣṭhitāṃ pratiṣṭhite vayasi saubhāgye ca duhitaram avasṛjanti gaṇikā iti prāpyopacārāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 1 2.2]
pāṇigrahaśca saṃvatsaram avyabhicāryas tato yathā kāminī syāt | [KāSū, 7, 1 2.3]
ūrdhvam api saṃvatsarāt pariṇītena nimantryamāṇā lābham apyutsṛjya tāṃ rātriṃ tasyāgacched iti veśyāyāḥ pāṇigrahaṇavidhiḥ saubhāgyavardhanaṃ ca | [KāSū, 7, 1 2.4]
etena raṅgopajīvināṃ kanyā vyākhyātāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 1 2.5]
tasmai tu tāṃ dadyur ya eṣāṃ tūryaviśiṣṭam upakuryāt | [KāSū, 7, 1 2.6]
iti subhagaṃkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 2.7]
dhattūrakamaricapippalīcūrṇair madhumiśrair liptaliṅgasya prayogo vaśīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.1]
vātodbhāntapatraṃ mṛtakanirmālyaṃ mayūrāsthicūrṇāvacūrṇaṃ vaśīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.2]
svayaṃmṛtāyā maṇḍalakārikāyāścūrṇaṃ madhusaṃyuktaṃ sahāmalakaiḥ snānaṃ vaśīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.3]
vajrasnuhīgaṇḍakāni khaṇḍaśaḥ kṛtāni manaḥśilāgandhapāṣāṇacūrṇenābhyajya saptakṛtvaḥ śoṣitāni cūrṇayitvā madhunā liptaliṅgasya saṃprayogo vaśīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.4]
etenaiva rātrau dhūmaṃ kṛtvā taddhūmatiraskṛtaṃ sauvarṇaṃ candramasaṃ darśayati | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.5]
etair eva cūrṇitair vānarapurīṣamiśritair yāṃ kanyām avakiret sānyasmai na dīyate | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.6]
vacāgaṇḍakāni sahakāratailaliptāni śiṃśapāvṛkṣaskandham utkīrya nidadhyāt | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.7]
ṣaḍbhir māsair apanītāni devakāntam anulepanaṃ vaśīkaraṇaṃ cetyācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.8]
tathā khadirasārajāni śakalāni tanūni yaṃ vṛkṣam utkīrya nidadhyāt tatpuṣpagandhāni bhavanti | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.9]
gandharvakāntam anulepanaṃ vaśīkaraṇaṃ cetyācakṣate priyaṃgavastagaramiśrāḥ sahakāratailadigdhā nāgakesaravṛkṣam utkīrya ṣaṇmāsanihitā nāgakāntam anulepanaṃ vaśīkaraṇam ityācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.10]
uṣṭrasyāsthi bhṛṅgarājarasena bhāvitaṃ dagdham añjanam uṣṭrāsthy añjanikāyāṃ nihitam uṣṭrāsthiśalākayaiva srotoñjanasahitaṃ puṇyaṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ vaśīkaraṇaṃ cetyācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.11]
etena śyenabhāsamayūrāsthimayānyañjanāni vyākhyātāni | [KāSū, 7, 1 3.12]
uccaṭākandaś ca yaṣṭīmadhukaṃ ca saśarkareṇa payasā pītvā vṛṣo bhavati | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.1]
meṣabastamuṣkasiddhasya payasaḥ saśarkarasya pānaṃ vṛṣatvayogaḥ | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.2]
tathā vidāryāḥ kṣīrikāyāḥ svayaṃguptāyāś ca kṣīreṇa pānam | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.3]
tathā piyālabījānāṃ moraṭākṣīravidāryośca kṣīreṇaiva | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.4]
śṛṅgāṭakakaserumadhūkāni kṣīrakākolyā saha piṣṭāni saśarkareṇa payasā ghṛtena mandāgninotkarikāṃ paktvā yāvadarthaṃ bhakṣitavān anantāḥ striyo gacchatīty ācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.5]
māṣakamalinīṃ payasā dhautām uṣṇena ghṛtena mṛdūkṛtyoddhṛtāṃ vṛddhavatsāyāḥ goḥ payaḥ siddhaṃ pāyasaṃ madhusarpirbhyām aśitvānantāḥ striyo gacchatīty ācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.6]
vidārī svayaṃguptā śarkarāmadhusarpirbhyāṃ godhūmacūrṇena polikāṃ kṛtvā yāvadarthaṃ bhakṣitavān anantāḥ striyo gacchatīty ācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.7]
caṭakāṇḍarasabhāvitaistaṇḍulaiḥ pāyasaṃ siddhaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ plāvitaṃ yāvadartham iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.8]
caṭakāṇḍarasabhāvitān apagatatvacastilān śṛṅgāṭakakaserukasvayaṃguptāphalāni godhūmamāṣacūrṇaiḥ saśarkareṇa payasā sarpiṣā ca pakvaṃ pāyasaṃ yāvadarthaṃ prāśitam iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.9]
sarpiṣo madhunaḥ śarkarāyā madhukasya ca dve dve pale madhurasāyāḥ karṣaḥ prasthaṃ payasa iti ṣaḍaṅgam amṛtaṃ medhyaṃ vṛṣyam āyuṣyaṃ yuktarasam ity ācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.10]
śatāvarīśvadaṃṣṭrāguḍakaṣāye pippalīmadhukalke gokṣīracchāgaghṛte pakve tasya puṣpārambheṇānvahaṃ prāśanaṃ medhyaṃ vṛṣyam āyuṣyaṃ yuktarasam ity ācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.11]
śatāvaryāḥ śvadaṃṣṭrāyāḥ śrīparṇīphalānāṃ ca kṣuṇṇānāṃ caturguṇe jale pāka ā prakṛtyavasthānāt | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.12]
śvadaṃṣṭrācūrṇasamanvitaṃ tatsamam eva yavacūrṇaṃ prātar utthāya dvipalikam anudinaṃ prāśnīyān medhyaṃ vṛṣyam āyuṣyaṃ yuktarasam ity ācakṣate | [KāSū, 7, 1 4.13]
āyurvedācca vedācca vidyātantrebhya eva ca | [KāSū, 7, 1 5.1]
āptebhyaścāvaboddhavyā yogā ye prītikārakāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 1 5.2]
na prayuñjīta saṃdigdhān na śarīrātyayāvahān | [KāSū, 7, 1 6.1]
na jīvaghātasambaddhān nāśucidravyasaṃyutān | [KāSū, 7, 1 6.2]
tathā yuktān prayuñjīta śiṣṭair api na ninditān | [KāSū, 7, 1 7.1]
brāhmaṇaiśca suhṛdbhiśca maṅgalair abhinanditān | [KāSū, 7, 1 7.2]
{KāSū, 7, 2}
caṇḍavegāṃ rañjayitum aśaknuvan yogān ācaret | [KāSū, 7, 2 1]
ratasyopakrame saṃbādhasya kareṇopamardanaṃ tasyā rasaprāptikāle ca ratayojanam iti rāgapratyānayanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 2]
aupariṣṭakaṃ mandavegasya gatavayaso vyāyatasya śrāntasya ca rāgapratyānayanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 3]
apadravyāṇi vā yojayet | [KāSū, 7, 2 4]
tāni suvarṇarajatatāmrakālāyasagajadantagavaladravyamayāṇi trāpuṣāṇi saisakāni ca mṛdūni śītavīryāṇi vṛṣyāṇi karmasahiṣṇūni bhavantīti bābhravīyā yogāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 5]
dārumayāni sāmyataśceti vātsyāyanaḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 6]
liṅgapramāṇāntaraṃ bindubhiḥ karkaśaparyantaṃ bahulaiḥ syāt | [KāSū, 7, 2 7]
eta eva dve saṃghāṭī | [KāSū, 7, 2 8]
triprabhṛti yāvatpramāṇaṃ vā cūḍakaḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 9]
ekām eva latikāṃ pramāṇavaśena veṣṭayed ityekacūḍakaḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 10]
ubhayatomukhacchidraḥ sthūlakarkaśapṛṣataguṭikāyuktaḥ pramāṇayogī kaṭhyāṃ baddhaḥ kañcuko jālakaṃ vā | [KāSū, 7, 2 11]
tadabhāve alābūnālakaṃ veṇuśca tailakaṣāyaiḥ subhāvitaḥ sūtrajaṅghābaddhaḥ ślakṣṇā kāṣṭhamālāl vā grathitā bahubhir āmalakāsthibhiḥ saṃyuktetyapaviddhayogāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 12]
na tvapaviddhasya kasyacid vyavahṛtir astīti dākṣiṇātyānāṃ liṅgasya karṇayor iva vyadhanaṃ bālasya | [KāSū, 7, 2 13]
yuvā tu śastreṇa chedayitvā yāvad rudhirasyāgamanaṃ tāvad udake tiṣṭhet | [KāSū, 7, 2 14]
vaiśadyārthaṃ ca tasyāṃ rātrau nirbandhād vyavāyaḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 15]
tataḥ kaṣāyair ekadināntaritaṃ śodhanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 16]
vetasakuṭajaśaṅkubhiḥ krameṇa vardhamānasya vardhanair bandhanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 17]
yaṣṭīmadhukena madhuyuktena śodhanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 18]
tataḥ sīsapatrakarṇikayā vardhayet | [KāSū, 7, 2 19]
mrakṣayed bhallātakataileneti vyadhanayogāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 20]
tasminn anekākṛtivikalpānyapadravyāṇi yojayet | [KāSū, 7, 2 21]
vṛttam ekato vṛttam udūkhalakaṃ kusumakaṃ kaṇṭakitaṃ kaṅkāsthigajaprahārikam aṣṭamaṇḍalikaṃ bhramarakaṃ śṛṅgāṭakam anyāni vopāyataḥ karmataśca bahukarmasahatā caiṣāṃ mṛdukarkaśatā yathā sātmyam iti naṣṭarāgapratyānayanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 22]
evaṃ vṛkṣajānāṃ jantūnāṃ śūkair upaliptaṃ liṅgaṃ daśarātraṃ tailena mṛditaṃ punaḥ punar upaliptaṃ punaḥ pramṛditam iti jātaśophaṃ khaṭvāyām adhomukhastad antare lambayet | [KāSū, 7, 2 23]
tataḥ śītaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ kṛtavedanānigrahaṃ sopakrameṇa niṣpādayet | [KāSū, 7, 2 24]
sa yāvajjīvaṃ śūkajo nāma śopho viṭānām | [KāSū, 7, 2 25]
aśvagandhāśabarakandajalaśūkabṛhatīphalamāhiṣanavanītahastikarṇavajravallīrasair ekaikena parimardanaṃ māsikaṃ vardhanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 26]
etair eva kaṣāyaiḥ pakvena tailena parimardanaṃ ṣaṇmāsyam | [KāSū, 7, 2 27]
dāḍimatrapusabījāni vālukaṃ bṛhatīphalarasaśceti mṛdvagninā pakvena tailena parimardanaṃ pariṣeko vā | [KāSū, 7, 2 28]
tāṃstāṃśca yogān āptebhyo budhyeteti vardhanayogāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 29]
snuhīkaṇṭakacūrṇaiḥ punarnavāvānarapurīṣalāṅgalikāmūlamiśrair yām avakiret sā nānyaṃ kāmayeta | [KāSū, 7, 2 30]
tathā somalatāvalgujabhṛṅgalohopajihvikācūrṇair vyādhighātakajambūphalarasaniryāsena ghanīkṛtena liptasaṃbādhāṃ gacchato rāgo naśyati | [KāSū, 7, 2 31]
gopālikābahupādikājihvikācūrṇair māhiṣatakrayuktaiḥ snāyāyāṃ gacchato rāgo naśyati | [KāSū, 7, 2 32]
nīpāmrātakajambūkusumayuktam anulepanaṃ daurbhāgyakaraṃ srajaśca | [KāSū, 7, 2 33]
kokilākṣaphalapralepo hastinyāḥ saṃhatam ekarātraṃ karoti | [KāSū, 7, 2 34]
padmotpalakandasarjakasugandhacūrṇāni madhunā piṣṭāni lepo mṛgyā viśālīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 2 35]
snuhīsomārkakṣīrair avalgujāphalair bhāvitānyāmalakāni keśānāṃ śvetīkaraṇam | [KāSū, 7, 2 36]
madayantikākuṭajakāñjanikāgirikarṇikāślakṣṇaparṇīmūlaiḥ snānāṃ keśapratyānayanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 37]
etair eva supakvena tailenābhyaṅgāt kṛṣṇīkaraṇaṃ krameṇāsya pratyānayanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 38]
śvetāśvasya muṣkasvedaiḥ saptakṛtvo bhāvitenālaktakena rakto 'dharaḥ śveto bhavati | [KāSū, 7, 2 39]
madayantikādīnyeva pratyānayanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 40]
bahupādikākuṣṭhatagaratālīśadevadāruvajrakandakair upaliptaṃ vaṃśaṃ vādayato yā śabdaṃ śṛṇoti sā vaśyā bhavati | [KāSū, 7, 2 41]
dhattūraphalayukto 'bhyavahāra unmādakaraḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 42]
guḍo jīrṇitaśca pratyānayanam | [KāSū, 7, 2 43]
haritālamanaḥśilābhakṣiṇo mayūrasya purīṣeṇa liptahasto yad dravyaṃ spṛśati tan na dṛśyate | [KāSū, 7, 2 44]
aṅgāratṛṇabhasmanā tailena vimiśram udakaṃ kṣīravarṇaṃ bhavati | [KāSū, 7, 2 45]
harītakyāmrātakayoḥ śravaṇapriyaṃgukābhiśca piṣṭābhir liptāni lohabhāṇḍāni tāmrībhavanti | [KāSū, 7, 2 46]
śravaṇapriyaṃgukātailena dukūlasarpanirmokeṇa vartyā dīpaṃ prajvālya pārśve dīrghīkṛtāni kāṣṭhāni sarpavad dṛśyante | [KāSū, 7, 2 47]
śvetāyāḥ śvetavatsāyā goḥ kṣīrasya pānaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam | [KāSū, 7, 2 48]
brāhmaṇānāṃ praśastān āmāśiṣaḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 49]
pūrvaśāstrāṇi saṃdṛśya prayogān upasṛtya ca | [KāSū, 7, 2 50.1]
kāmasūtram idaṃ yatnāt saṃkṣepeṇa nirveśitam | [KāSū, 7, 2 50.2]
dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca pratyayaṃ lokam eva ca | [KāSū, 7, 2 51.1]
paśyatyetasya tattvajño na ca rāgāt pravartate | [KāSū, 7, 2 51.2]
adhikāravaśād uktā ye citrā rāgavardhanāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 52.1]
tadanantaram atraiva te yatnād vinivāritāḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 52.2]
na śāstram astītyetena prayogo hi samīkṣyate | [KāSū, 7, 2 53.1]
śāstrārthān vyāpino vidyāt prayogāṃstv ekadeśikān | [KāSū, 7, 2 53.2]
bābhravīyāṃśca sūtrārthān āgamaṃ suvimṛśya ca | [KāSū, 7, 2 54.1]
vātsyāyanaścakāredaṃ kāmasūtraṃ yathāvidhi | [KāSū, 7, 2 54.2]
tad etad brahmacaryeṇa pareṇa ca samādhinā | [KāSū, 7, 2 55.1]
vihitaṃ lokayātrāyai na rāgārtho 'sya saṃvidhiḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 55.2]
rakṣandharmārthakāmānāṃ sthitiṃ svāṃ lokavartinīm | [KāSū, 7, 2 56.1]
asya śāstrasya tattvajño bhavatyeva jitendriyaḥ | [KāSū, 7, 2 56.2]
tad etat kuśalo vidvān dharmārthāvavalokayan | [KāSū, 7, 2 57.1]
nātirāgātmakaḥ kāmī prayuñjānaḥ prasidhyati | [KāSū, 7, 2 57.2]
